#Text:Gopathabrāhmaṇa
#Edition:Gastra (DCS version)
#Data entry:A. Griffiths



1.1.1.1	oṃ brahma ha vā idam agra āsīt svayaṃbhv ekam eva
1.1.1.2	tadaikṣata
1.1.1.3	mahad vai yakṣam yad ekam evāsmi
1.1.1.4	hantāhaṃ mad eva manmātraṃ dvitīyaṃ devaṃ nirmimā iti
1.1.1.5	tad abhyaśrāmyad abhyatapat samatapat
1.1.1.6	tasya śrāntasya taptasya saṃtaptasya lalāṭe sneho yad ārdram ājāyata
1.1.1.7	tenānandat
1.1.1.8	tad abravīt
1.1.1.9	mahad vai yakṣaṃ suvedam avidam aham iti
1.1.1.10	tad yad abravīt
1.1.1.11	mahad vai yakṣaṃ suvedam avidam aham iti
1.1.1.12	tasmāt suvedo 'bhavat
1.1.1.13	taṃ vā etaṃ suvedaṃ santaṃ sveda ity ācakṣate parokṣeṇa
1.1.1.14	parokṣapriyā iva hi devā bhavanti pratyakṣadviṣaḥ
1.1.2.1	sa bhūyo 'śrāmyad bhūyo 'tapyad bhūya ātmānaṃ samatapat
1.1.2.2	tasya śrāntasya taptasya saṃtaptasya sarvebhyo romagartebhyaḥ pṛthaksvedadhārāḥ prāsyandanta
1.1.2.3	tābhir anandat
1.1.2.4	tad abravīt
1.1.2.5	ābhir vā aham idaṃ sarvaṃ dhārayiṣyāmi yad idaṃ kiṃ ca
1.1.2.6	ābhir vā aham idaṃ sarvaṃ janayiṣyāmi yad idaṃ kiṃ ca
1.1.2.7	ābhir vā aham idaṃ sarvaṃ āpsyāmi yad idaṃ kiṃ ceti
1.1.2.8	tad yad abravīt
1.1.2.9	ābhir vā aham idaṃ sarvaṃ dhārayiṣyāmi yad idaṃ kiṃ ceti
1.1.2.10	tasmād dhārā abhavan
1.1.2.11	tad dhārāṇāṃ dhārātvaṃ yac cāsu dhriyate
1.1.2.12	tad yad abravīt
1.1.2.13	ābhir vā aham idaṃ sarvaṃ janayiṣyāmi yad idaṃ kiṃ ceti
1.1.2.14	tasmāj jāyā abhavan
1.1.2.15	taj jāyānāṃ jāyātvaṃ yac cāsu puruṣo jāyate yac ca putraḥ
1.1.2.16	pun nāma narakam anekaśatatāram
1.1.2.17	tasmāt trātīti putraḥ
1.1.2.18	tat putrasya putratvam
1.1.2.19	tad yad abravīt
1.1.2.20	ābhir vā aham idaṃ sarvaṃ āpsyāmi yad idaṃ kiṃ ceti
1.1.2.21	tasmād āpo 'bhavan
1.1.2.22	tad apām aptvam
1.1.2.23	āpnoti vai sa sarvān kāmān yān kāmayate
1.1.3.1	tā apaḥ sṛṣṭvānvaikṣata
1.1.3.2	tāsu svāṃ chāyām apaśyat
1.1.3.3	tām asyekṣamāṇasya svayaṃ reto 'skandat
1.1.3.4	tad apsu pratyatiṣṭhat
1.1.3.5	tās tatraivābhyaśrāmyad abhyatapat samatapat
1.1.3.6	tāḥ śrāntās taptāḥ saṃtaptāḥ sārdham eva retasā dvaidham abhavan
1.1.3.7	tāsām anyatarā atilavaṇā apeyā asvādvyaḥ
1.1.3.8	tā aśāntā retaḥ samudraṃ vṛtvātiṣṭhan
1.1.3.9	athetarāḥ peyāḥ svādvyaḥ śāntāḥ
1.1.3.10	tās tatraivābhyaśrāmyad abhyatapat samatapat
1.1.3.11	tābhyaḥ śrāntābhyas taptābhyaḥ saṃtaptābhyo yad reta āsīt tad abhṛjjyata
1.1.3.12	tasmād bhṛguḥ samabhavat
1.1.3.13	tad bhṛgor bhṛgutvam
1.1.3.14	bhṛgur iva vai sa sarveṣu lokeṣu bhāti ya evaṃ veda
1.1.4.1	sa bhṛguṃ sṛṣṭvāntaradhīyata
1.1.4.2	sa bhṛguḥ sṛṣṭaḥ prāṅ aijata
1.1.4.3	taṃ vāg anvavadat
1.1.4.4	vāyo vāya iti
1.1.4.5	sa nyavartata sa dakṣiṇāṃ diśam aijata
1.1.4.6	taṃ vāg anvavadat
1.1.4.7	mātariśvan mātariśvann iti
1.1.4.8	sa nyavartata sa pratīcīṃ diśam aijata
1.1.4.9	taṃ vāg anvavadat
1.1.4.10	pavamāna pavamāneti
1.1.4.11	sa nyavartata sa udīcīṃ diśam aijata
1.1.4.12	taṃ vāg anvavadat
1.1.4.13	vāta vāteti
1.1.4.14	tam abravīt
1.1.4.15	na nv avidam aham iti
1.1.4.16	na hīti
1.1.4.17	athārvāṅ enam etāsv evāpsv anviccheti
1.1.4.18	tad yad abravīd athārvāṅ enam etāsv evāpsv anviccheti tad atharvābhavat
1.1.4.19	tad atharvaṇo 'tharvatvam
1.1.4.20	tasya ha vā etasya bhagavato 'tharvaṇa ṛṣer yathaiva brahmaṇo lomāni yathāṅgāni yathā prāṇa evam evāsya sarva ātmā samabhavat
1.1.4.21	tam atharvāṇaṃ brahmābravīt prajāpateḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā pālayasveti
1.1.4.22	tad yad abravīt prajāpateḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā pālayasveti tasmāt prajāpatir abhavat
1.1.4.23	tat prajāpateḥ prajāpatitvam
1.1.4.24	atharvā vai prajāpatiḥ
1.1.4.25	prajāpatir iva vai sa sarveṣu lokeṣu bhāti ya evaṃ veda
1.1.5.1	tam atharvāṇam ṛṣim abhyaśrāmyad abhyatapat samatapat
1.1.5.2	tasmācchrāntāttaptāt saṃtaptād daśatayān atharvaṇa ṛṣīn niramimataikarcān dvyṛcāṃs tṛcāṃścaturṛcān pañcarcānt ṣaḍarcānt saptarcān aṣṭarcān navarcān daśarcān iti
1.1.5.3	tān atharvaṇa ṛṣīn abhyaśrāmyad abhyatapat samatapat
1.1.5.4	tebhyaḥ śrāntebhyas taptebhyaḥ saṃtaptebhyo daśatayān ātharvaṇān ārṣeyān niramimataikādaśān dvādaśāṃs trayodaśāṃś caturdaśān pañcadaśān ṣoḍaśānt saptadaśān aṣṭādaśān navadaśān viṃśān iti
1.1.5.5	tān atharvaṇa ṛṣīn ātharvaṇāṃś cārṣeyān abhyaśrāmyad abhyatapat samatapat
1.1.5.6	tebhyaḥ śrāntebhyas taptebhyaḥ saṃtaptebhyo yān mantrān apaśyat sa ātharvaṇo vedo 'bhavat
1.1.5.7	tam ātharvaṇaṃ vedam abhyaśrāmyad abhyatapat samatapat
1.1.5.8	tasmācchrāntāttaptātsaṃtaptād omiti mana evordhvam akṣaram udakrāmat
1.1.5.9	sa ya icchet sarvair etair atharvabhiś cātharvaṇaiś ca kurvīyety etayaiva tan mahāvyāhṛtyā kurvīta
1.1.5.10	sarvair ha vā asyaitair atharvabhiś cātharvaṇaiś ca kṛtaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda yaś caivaṃ vidvān evam etayā mahāvyāhṛtyā kurute
1.1.6.1	sa bhūyo 'śrāmyad bhūyo 'tapyad bhūya ātmānaṃ samatapat
1.1.6.2	sa ātmata eva trīṃl lokān niramimīta pṛthivīm antarikṣaṃ divam iti
1.1.6.3	sa khalu pādābhyām eva pṛthivīṃ niramimīta
1.1.6.4	udarād antarikṣaṃ mūrdhno divam
1.1.6.5	sa tāṃs trīṃllokān abhyaśrāmyad abhyatapat samatapat
1.1.6.6	tebhyaḥ śrāntebhyas taptebhyaḥ saṃtaptebhyas trīn devān niramimīta
1.1.6.7	agniṃ vāyum ādityam iti
1.1.6.8	sa khalu pṛthivyā evāgniṃ niramimītāntarikṣād vāyuṃ diva ādityam
1.1.6.9	sa tāṃs trīn devān abhyaśrāmyad abhyatapat samatapat
1.1.6.10	tebhyaḥ śrāntebhyas taptebhyaḥ saṃtaptebhyas trīn vedān niramimīta ṛgvedaṃ yajurvedaṃ sāmavedam iti
1.1.6.11	agner ṛgvedaṃ vāyor yajurvedaṃ ādityāt sāmavedam
1.1.6.12	sa tāṃs trīn vedān abhyaśrāmyad abhyatapat samatapat
1.1.6.13	tebhyaḥ śrāntebhyas taptebhyaḥ saṃtaptebhyas tisro mahāvyāhṛtīr niramimīta bhūr bhuvaḥ svar iti
1.1.6.14	bhūr ity ṛgvedād bhuva iti yajurvedāt svar iti sāmavedāt
1.1.6.15	sa ya icchet sarvair etais tribhir vedaiḥ kurvīyety etābhir eva tan mahāvyāhṛtibhiḥ kurvīta
1.1.6.16	sarvair ha vā asyaitais tribhir vedaiḥ kṛtaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda yaś caivaṃ vidvān evam etābhir mahāvyāhṛtibhiḥ kurute
1.1.7.1	tā yā amū retaḥ samudraṃ vṛtvātiṣṭhaṃs tāḥ prācyo dakṣiṇācyaḥ pratīcya udīcyaḥ samavadravanta
1.1.7.2	tad yat samavadravanta tasmāt samudra ucyate
1.1.7.3	tā bhītā abruvan
1.1.7.4	bhagavantam eva vayaṃ rājānaṃ vṛṇīmaha iti
1.1.7.5	yac ca vṛtvātiṣṭhaṃs tad varaṇo 'bhavat
1.1.7.6	taṃ vā etaṃ varaṇaṃ santaṃ varuṇa ity ācakṣate parokṣeṇa
1.1.7.7	parokṣapriyā iva hi devā bhavanti pratyakṣadviṣaḥ
1.1.7.8	sa samudrād amucyata
1.1.7.9	sa mucyur abhavat
1.1.7.10	taṃ vā etaṃ mucyuṃ santaṃ mṛtyur ity ācakṣate parokṣeṇa
1.1.7.11	parokṣapriyā iva hi devā bhavanti pratyakṣadviṣaḥ
1.1.7.12	taṃ varuṇaṃ mṛtyum abhyaśrāmyad abhyatapat samatapat
1.1.7.13	tasya śrāntasya taptasya saṃtaptasya sarvebhyo 'ṅgebhyo raso 'kṣarat
1.1.7.14	so 'ṅgaraso 'bhavat
1.1.7.15	taṃ vā etaṃ aṅgarasaṃ santam aṅgirā ity ācakṣate parokṣeṇa
1.1.7.16	parokṣapriyā iva hi devā bhavanti pratyakṣadviṣaḥ
1.1.8.1	tam aṅgirasam ṛṣim abhyaśrāmyad abhyatapat samatapat
1.1.8.2	tasmācchrāntāt taptāt saṃtaptād viṃśino 'ṅgirasa ṛṣīn niramimīta
1.1.8.3	tān viṃśino 'ṅgirasa ṛṣīn abhyaśrāmyad abhyatapat samatapat
1.1.8.4	tebhyaḥ śrāntebhyas taptebhyaḥ saṃtaptebhyo daśatayān āṅgirasān ārṣeyān niramimīta ṣoḍaśino 'ṣṭādaśino dvādaśina ekarcān dvyṛcāṃs tṛcāṃś caturṛcān pañcarcān ṣaḍarcān saptarcān iti
1.1.8.5	tān aṅgirasa ṛṣīn āṅgirasāṃś cārṣeyān abhyaśrāmyad abhyatapat samatapat
1.1.8.6	tebhyaḥ śrāntebhyas taptebhyaḥ saṃtaptebhyo yān mantrān apaśyat sa āṅgiraso vedo 'bhavat
1.1.8.7	tām āṅgirasaṃ vedam abhyaśrāmyad abhyatapat samatapat
1.1.8.8	tasmācchrāntāt taptāt saṃtaptāj janad iti dvaitam akṣaraṃ vyabhavat
1.1.8.9	sa ya icchet sarvair etair aṅgirobhiś cāṅgirasaiś ca kurvīyety etayaiva tan mahāvyāhṛtyā kurvīta
1.1.8.10	sarvair ha vā asyaitairaṅgirobhiścāṅgirasaiśca kṛtaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda yaś caivaṃ vidvān evam etayā mahāvyāhṛtyā kurute
1.1.9.1	sa ūrdhvo 'tiṣṭhat
1.1.9.2	sa imāṃllokān vyaṣṭabhnāt
1.1.9.3	tasmād aṅgiraso 'dhīyāna ūrdhvas tiṣṭhati
1.1.9.4	tad vrataṃ sa manasā dhyāyed yad vā ahaṃ kiṃ ca manasā dhyāsyāmi tathaiva tad bhaviṣyati
1.1.9.5	taddha sma tathaiva bhavati
1.1.9.6	tadapyetadṛcoktam
1.1.9.7	śreṣṭho ha vedas tapaso 'dhi jāto brahmajyānāṃ kṣitaye saṃbabhūva
1.1.9.8	ṛjyad bhūtaṃ yad asṛjyatedaṃ niveśanam anṛṇaṃ dūram asyeti
1.1.9.9	tā vā etā aṅgirasāṃ jāmayo yan menayaḥ
1.1.9.10	karoti menibhir vīryaṃ ya evaṃ veda
1.1.10.1	sa diśo 'nvaikṣata prācīṃ dakṣiṇāṃ pratīcīm udīcīṃ dhruvām ūrdhvām iti
1.1.10.2	tās tatraivābhyaśrāmyad abhyatapat samatapat
1.1.10.3	tābhyaḥ śrāntābhyas taptābhyaḥ saṃtaptābhyaḥ pañca vedān niramimīta
1.1.10.4	sarpavedaṃ piśācavedam asuravedam itihāsavedaṃ purāṇavedam iti
1.1.10.5	sa khalu prācyā eva diśaḥ sarpavedaṃ niramimīta
1.1.10.6	dakṣiṇasyāḥ piśācavedam
1.1.10.7	pratīcyā asuravedam
1.1.10.8	udīcyā itihāsavedam
1.1.10.9	dhruvāyāś cordhvāyāś ca purāṇavedam
1.1.10.10	sa tān pañca vedān abhyaśrāmyad abhyatapat samatapat
1.1.10.11	tebhyaḥ śrāntebhyas taptebhyaḥ saṃtaptebhyaḥ pañca mahāvyāhṛtīr niramimīta
1.1.10.12	vṛdhat karad ruhan mahat tad iti
1.1.10.13	vṛdhad iti sarpavedāt
1.1.10.14	karad iti piśācavedāt
1.1.10.15	ruhad ity asuravedāt
1.1.10.16	mahad itītihāsavedāt
1.1.10.17	tad iti purāṇavedāt
1.1.10.18	sa ya icchet sarvair etaiḥ pañcabhir vedaiḥ kurvīyety etābhir eva tan mahāvyāhṛtibhiḥ kurvīta
1.1.10.19	sarvair ha vā asyaitaiḥ pañcabhir vedaiḥ kṛtaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda yaś caivaṃ vidvān evam etābhir mahāvyāhṛtibhiḥ kurute
1.1.11.1	sa āvataś ca parāvataś cānvaikṣata
1.1.11.2	tās tatraivābhyaśrāmyad abhyatapat samatapat
1.1.11.3	tābhyaḥ śrāntābhyas taptābhyaḥ saṃtaptābhyaḥ śam ity ūrdhvam akṣaram udakrāmat
1.1.11.4	sa ya icchet sarvābhir etābhir āvadbhiś ca parāvadbhiś ca kurvīyety etayaiva tan mahāvyāhṛtyā kurvīta
1.1.11.5	sarvābhir ha vā asyaitābhir āvadbhiś ca parāvadbhiś ca kṛtaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda yaś caivaṃ vidvān evam etayā mahāvyāhṛtyā kurute
1.1.12.1	sa bhūyo 'śrāmyad bhūyo 'tapyad bhūya ātmānaṃ samatapat
1.1.12.2	sa manasa eva candramasaṃ niramimīta
1.1.12.3	nakhebhyo nakṣatrāṇi
1.1.12.4	lomabhya oṣadhivanaspatīn
1.1.12.5	kṣudrebhyaḥ prāṇebhyo 'nyān bahūn devān
1.1.12.6	sa bhūyo 'śrāmyad bhūyo 'tapyad bhūya ātmānaṃ samatapat
1.1.12.7	sa etaṃ trivṛtaṃ saptatantum ekaviṃśatisaṃsthaṃ yajñam apaśyat
1.1.12.8	tad apy etad ṛcoktam
1.1.12.9	agnir yajñaṃ trivṛtaṃ saptatantum iti
1.1.12.10	athāpy eṣa prākrīḍitaḥ ślokaḥ pratyabhivadati
1.1.12.11	sapta sutyāḥ sapta ca pākayajñā iti
1.1.13.1	tam āharat
1.1.13.2	tenāyajata
1.1.13.3	tasyāgnir hotāsīt
1.1.13.4	vāyur adhvaryuḥ
1.1.13.5	sūrya udgātā
1.1.13.6	candramā brahmā
1.1.13.7	parjanyaḥ sadasyaḥ
1.1.13.8	oṣadhivanaspatayaś camasādhvaryavaḥ
1.1.13.9	viśve devā hotrakāḥ
1.1.13.10	atharvāṅgiraso goptāraḥ
1.1.13.11	taṃ ha smaitam evaṃ vidvāṃsaḥ pūrve śrotriyā yajñaṃ tataṃ sāvasāya ha smāhety abhivrajanti
1.1.13.12	mā no 'yaṃ gharma udyataḥ pramattānām amṛtāḥ prajāḥ pradhākṣīd iti
1.1.13.13	tān vā etān parirakṣakānt sadaḥprasarpakān ity ācakṣate dakṣiṇāsamṛddhān
1.1.13.14	tad u ha smāha prajāpatiḥ
1.1.13.15	yad vai yajñe 'kuśalā ṛtvijo bhavanty acaritino brahmacaryam aparāgyā vā
1.1.13.16	tad vai yajñasya viriṣṭam ity ācakṣate
1.1.13.17	yajñasya viriṣṭam anu yajamāno viriṣyate
1.1.13.18	yajamānasya viriṣṭam anv ṛtvijo viriṣyante
1.1.13.19	ṛtvijāṃ viriṣṭam anu dakṣiṇā viriṣyante
1.1.13.20	dakṣiṇānāṃ viriṣṭam anu yajamānaḥ putrapaśubhir viriṣyate
1.1.13.21	putrapaśūnāṃ viriṣṭam anu yajamānaḥ svargeṇa lokena viriṣyate
1.1.13.22	svargasya lokasya viriṣṭam anu tasyārdhasya yogakṣemo viriṣyate yasminn ardhe yajanta iti brāhmaṇam
1.1.14.1	taṃ ha smaitam evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brahmāṇaṃ yajñaviriṣṭī vā yajñaviriṣṭino vety upādhāveran
1.1.14.2	namas te astu bhagavan
1.1.14.3	yajñasya no viriṣṭaṃ saṃdhehīti
1.1.14.4	tad yatraiva viriṣṭaṃ syāt tatrāgnīn upasamādhāya śāntyudakaṃ kṛtvā pṛthivyai śrotrāyeti trir evāgnīnt samprokṣati triḥ paryukṣati
1.1.14.5	triḥ kārayamānam ācāmayati ca samprokṣati ca
1.1.14.6	yajñavāstu ca samprokṣati
1.1.14.7	athāpi vedānāṃ rasena yajñasya viriṣṭaṃ saṃdhīyate
1.1.14.8	tad yathā lavaṇena suvarṇaṃ saṃdadhyāt suvarṇena rajataṃ rajatena lohaṃ lohena sīsaṃ sīsena trapv evam evāsya yajñasya viriṣṭaṃ saṃdhīyate
1.1.14.9	yajñasya saṃdhitim anu yajamānaḥ saṃdhīyate
1.1.14.10	yajamānasya saṃdhitim anv ṛtvijaḥ saṃdhīyante
1.1.14.11	ṛtvijāṃ saṃdhitim anu dakṣiṇāḥ saṃdhīyante
1.1.14.12	dakṣiṇānāṃ saṃdhitim anu yajamānaḥ putrapaśubhiḥ saṃdhīyate
1.1.14.13	putrapaśūnāṃ saṃdhitim anu yajamānaḥ svargeṇa lokena saṃdhīyate
1.1.14.14	svargasya lokasya saṃdhitim anu tasyārdhasya yogakṣemaḥ saṃdhīyate yasminn ardhe yajanta iti brāhmaṇam
1.1.15.1	tad u ha smāhātharvā devo vijānan yajñaviriṣṭānandānīty upaśamayeran yajñe prāyaścittiḥ kriyate 'pi ca yad u bahv iva yajñe vilomaṃ kriyate na caivāsya kācanārtir bhavati na ca yajñaviṣkandham upayāty apahanti punarmṛtyum apātyeti punarājātiṃ kāmacāro 'sya sarveṣu lokeṣu bhāti ya evaṃ veda yaś caivaṃ vidvān brahmā bhavati yasya caivaṃ vidvān brahmā dakṣiṇataḥ sado 'dhyāste yasya caivaṃ vidvān brahmā dakṣiṇata udaṅmukha āsīno yajña ājyāhutīr juhotīti brāhmaṇam
1.1.16.1	brahma ha vai brahmāṇaṃ puṣkare sasṛje

1.1.16.3	kenāham ekenākṣareṇa sarvāṃś ca kāmānt sarvāṃś ca lokānt sarvāṃś ca devānt sarvāṃś ca vedānt sarvāṃś ca yajñānt sarvāṃś ca śabdānt sarvāś ca vyuṣṭīḥ sarvāṇi ca bhūtāni sthāvarajaṅgamāny anubhaveyam iti

1.1.16.6	tayā sarvāṃś ca kāmānt sarvāṃś ca lokānt sarvāṃś ca devānt sarvāṃś ca vedānt sarvāṃś ca yajñānt sarvāṃś ca śabdānt sarvāś ca vyuṣṭīḥ sarvāṇi ca bhūtāni sthāvarajaṅgamāny anvabhavat

1.1.17.1	tasya prathamayā svaramātrayā pṛthivīm agnim oṣadhivanaspatīn ṛgvedaṃ bhūr iti vyāhṛtiṃ gāyatraṃ chandas trivṛtaṃ stomaṃ prācīṃ diśaṃ vasantam ṛtuṃ vācam adhyātmaṃ jihvāṃ rasam itīndriyāṇy anvabhavat
1.1.18.1	tasya dvitīyayā svaramātrayāntarikṣaṃ vāyuṃ yajurvedaṃ bhuva iti vyāhṛtiṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ chandaḥ pañcadaśaṃ stomaṃ pratīcīṃ diśaṃ grīṣmam ṛtuṃ prāṇam adhyātmaṃ nāsike gandhaghrāṇam itīndriyāṇy anvabhavat
1.1.19.1	tasya tṛtīyayā svaramātrayā divam ādityaṃ sāmavedaṃ svar iti vyāhṛtiṃ jāgataṃ chandaḥ saptadaśaṃ stomam udīcīṃ diśaṃ varṣā ṛtuṃ jyotir adhyātmaṃ cakṣuṣī darśanam itīndriyāny anvabhavat

1.1.21.1	tasya makāraśrutyetihāsapurāṇaṃ vākovākyaṃ gāthā nārāśaṃsīr upaniṣado 'nuśāsanānīti vṛdhat karad ruhan mahat tac cham om iti vyāhṛtīḥ svaraśamyanānātantrīḥ svaranṛtyagītavāditrāṇy anvabhavac caitrarathaṃ daivataṃ vaidyutaṃ jyotir bārhataṃ chandas triṇavatrayastriṃśau stomau dhruvām ūrdhvāṃ diśaṃ hemantaśiśirāv ṛtū śrotram adhyātmaṃ śabdaśravaṇam itīndriyāṇy anvabhavat

1.1.31.14	bho iti
1.1.31.15	yan nu khalu saumyāsmābhiḥ sarve vedā mukhato gṛhītāḥ kathaṃ ta evam ācāryo bhāṣate
1.1.31.16	kathaṃ nu śiṣṭāḥ śiṣṭebhya evaṃ bhāṣeran
1.1.31.17	yaṃ hy enam ahaṃ praśnaṃ pṛcchāmi na taṃ vivakṣyati
1.1.31.18	na hy enam adhyetīti
1.1.31.19	sa ha maudgalyaḥ svam antevāsinam uvāca parehi saumya glāvaṃ maitreyam upasīda
1.1.31.20	adhīhi bhoḥ sāvitrīṃ gāyatrīṃ caturviṃśatiyoniṃ dvādaśamithunām
1.1.31.21	yasyā bhṛgvaṅgirasaś cakṣuḥ
1.1.31.22	yasyāṃ sarvam idaṃ śritaṃ tāṃ bhavān prabravītv iti
1.1.31.23	sa cet saumya duradhīyāno bhaviṣyaty ācāryovāca brahmacārī brahmacāriṇo sāvitrīṃ prāheti vakṣyati tat tvaṃ brūyād duradhīyānaṃ taṃ vai bhavān maudgalyam avocat
1.1.31.24	sa tvā yaṃ praśnam aprākṣīn na taṃ vyavocaḥ
1.1.31.25	purā saṃvatsarād ārtim āriṣyasīti
1.1.32.1	sa tatrājagāma yatretaro babhūva
1.1.32.2	taṃ ha papraccha
1.1.32.3	sa ha na pratipede
1.1.32.4	taṃ hovāca duradhīyānaṃ taṃ vai bhavān maudgalyam avocat
1.1.32.5	sa tvā yaṃ praśnam aprākṣīn na taṃ vyavocaḥ
1.1.32.6	purā saṃvatsarād ārtim āriṣyasīti
1.1.32.7	sa ha maitreyaḥ svān antevāsina uvāca yathārthaṃ bhavanto yathāgṛhaṃ yathāmano viprasṛjyantām
1.1.32.8	duradhīyānaṃ vā ahaṃ maudgalyam avocam
1.1.32.9	sa mā yaṃ praśnam aprākṣīn na taṃ vyavocam
1.1.32.10	tam upaiṣyāmi
1.1.32.11	śāntiṃ kariṣyāmīti
1.1.32.12	sa ha maitreyaḥ prātaḥ samitpāṇir maudgalyam upasasādāsau vā ahaṃ bho maitreyaḥ
1.1.32.13	kimartham iti
1.1.32.14	duradhīyānaṃ vā ahaṃ bhavantam avocam
1.1.32.15	tvaṃ mā yaṃ praśnam aprākṣīr na taṃ vyavocam
1.1.32.16	tvām upaiṣyāmi
1.1.32.17	śāntiṃ kariṣyāmīti
1.1.32.18	sa hovācātra vā upetaṃ ca sarvaṃ ca kṛtaṃ pāpakena tvā yānena carantam āhuḥ
1.1.32.19	atho 'yaṃ mama kalyāṇaḥ
1.1.32.20	taṃ te dadāmi
1.1.32.21	tena yāhīti
1.1.32.22	sa hovācaitad evātrātviṣaṃ cānṛśaṃsyaṃ ca yathā bhavān āha
1.1.32.23	upāyāmi tveva bhavantam iti
1.1.32.24	taṃ hopeyāya
1.1.32.25	taṃ hopetya papraccha kiṃ svid āhur bhoḥ savitur vareṇyaṃ bhargo devasya kavayaḥ kim āhur dhiyo vicakṣva yadi tāḥ pravettha
1.1.32.26	pracodayāt savitā yābhir etīti
1.1.32.27	tasmā etat provāca vedāṃś chandāṃsi savitur vareṇyam
1.1.32.28	bhargo devasya kavayo 'nnam āhuḥ karmāṇi dhiyaḥ
1.1.32.29	tad u te prabravīmi pracodayāt savitā yābhir etīti
1.1.32.30	tam upasaṃgṛhya papracchādhīhi bhoḥ kaḥ savitā kā sāvitrī
1.1.33.1	mana eva savitā vāk sāvitrī
1.1.33.2	yatra hy eva manas tad vāg yatra vai vāk tan mana iti
1.1.33.3	ete dve yonī ekaṃ mithunam
1.1.33.4	agnir eva savitā pṛthivī sāvitrī
1.1.33.5	yatra hy evāgnis tat pṛthivī yatra vai pṛthivī tad agnir iti
1.1.33.6	ete dve yonī ekaṃ mithunam
1.1.33.7	vāyur eva savitāntarikṣaṃ sāvitrī
1.1.33.8	yatra hy eva vāyus tad antarikṣaṃ yatra vā antarikṣaṃ tad vāyur iti
1.1.33.9	ete dve yonī ekaṃ mithunam
1.1.33.10	āditya eva savitā dyauḥ sāvitrī
1.1.33.11	yatra hy evādityas tad dyaur yatra vai dyaus tad āditya iti
1.1.33.12	ete dve yonī ekaṃ mithunam
1.1.33.13	candramā eva savitā nakṣatrāṇi sāvitrī
1.1.33.14	yatra hy eva candramās tan nakṣatrāṇi yatra vai nakṣatrāṇi tac candramā iti
1.1.33.15	ete dve yonī ekaṃ mithunam
1.1.33.16	ahar eva savitā rātriḥ sāvitrī
1.1.33.17	yatra hy evāhas tad rātrir yatra vai rātris tad ahar iti
1.1.33.18	ete dve yonī ekaṃ mithunam
1.1.33.19	uṣṇam eva savitā śītaṃ sāvitrī
1.1.33.20	yatra hy evoṣṇaṃ tac chītaṃ yatra vai śītaṃ tad uṣṇam iti
1.1.33.21	ete dve yonī ekaṃ mithunam
1.1.33.22	abhram eva savitā varṣaṃ sāvitrī
1.1.33.23	yatra hy evābhraṃ tad varṣaṃ yatra vai varṣaṃ tad abhram iti
1.1.33.24	ete dve yonī ekaṃ mithunam
1.1.33.25	vidyud eva savitā stanayitnuḥ sāvitrī
1.1.33.26	yatra hy eva vidyut tat stanayitnur yatra vai stanayitnus tad vidyud iti
1.1.33.27	ete dve yonī ekaṃ mithunam
1.1.33.28	prāṇa eva savitānnaṃ sāvitrī
1.1.33.29	yatra hy eva prāṇas tad annaṃ yatra vā annaṃ tat prāṇa iti
1.1.33.30	ete dve yonī ekaṃ mithunam
1.1.33.31	vedā eva savitā chandāṃsi sāvitrī
1.1.33.32	yatra hy eva vedās tac chandāṃsi yatra vai chandāṃsi tad vedā iti
1.1.33.33	ete dve yonī ekaṃ mithunam
1.1.33.34	yajña eva savitā dakṣiṇāḥ sāvitrī
1.1.33.35	yatra hy eva yajñas tad dakṣiṇā yatra vai dakṣiṇās tad yajña iti
1.1.33.36	ete dve yonī ekaṃ mithunam
1.1.33.37	etaddha smaitad vidvāṃsam opākārim āsastur brahmacārī te saṃsthita ity athaita āsastur ācita iva cito babhūva
1.1.33.38	athotthāya prāvrājīd ity etad vā ahaṃ veda naitāsu yoniṣv ita etebhyo vā mithunebhyaḥ sambhūto brahmacārī mama purāyuṣaḥ preyād iti
1.1.34.1	brahma hedaṃ śriyaṃ pratiṣṭhām āyatanam aikṣata
1.1.34.2	tat tapasva
1.1.34.3	yadi tad vrate dhriyeta tat satye pratyatiṣṭhat
1.1.34.4	sa savitā sāvitryā brāhmaṇaṃ sṛṣṭvā tat sāvitrīṃ paryadadhāt
1.1.34.5	tat savitur vareṇyam iti sāvitryāḥ prathamaḥ pādaḥ
1.1.34.6	pṛthivyarcaṃ samadadhāt
1.1.34.7	ṛcāgnim
1.1.34.8	agninā śriyam
1.1.34.9	śriyā striyam
1.1.34.10	striyā mithunam
1.1.34.11	mithunena prajām
1.1.34.12	prajayā karma
1.1.34.13	karmaṇā tapaḥ
1.1.34.14	tapasā satyam
1.1.34.15	satyena brahma
1.1.34.16	brahmaṇā brāhmaṇam
1.1.34.17	brāhmaṇena vratam
1.1.34.18	vratena vai brāhmaṇaḥ saṃśito bhavati
1.1.34.19	aśūnyo bhavaty avicchinno bhavaty avicchinno 'sya tantur avicchinnaṃ jīvanaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda yaś caivaṃ vidvān evam etaṃ sāvitryāḥ prathamaṃ pādaṃ vyācaṣṭe
1.1.35.1	bhargo devasya dhīmahīti sāvitryā dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ
1.1.35.2	antarikṣeṇa yajuḥ samadadhāt
1.1.35.3	yajuṣā vāyum
1.1.35.4	vāyunābhram
1.1.35.5	abhreṇa varṣam
1.1.35.6	varṣeṇauṣadhivanaspatīn
1.1.35.7	oṣadhivanaspatibhiḥ paśūn
1.1.35.8	paśubhiḥ karma
1.1.35.9	karmaṇā tapaḥ

1.1.35.12	brahmaṇā brāhmaṇam

1.1.35.15	aśūnyo bhavaty avicchinno bhavaty avicchinno 'sya tantur avicchinnaṃ jīvanaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda yaś caivaṃ vidvān evam etaṃ sāvitryā dvitīyaṃ pādaṃ vyācaṣṭe
1.1.36.1	dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayād iti sāvitryās tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ
1.1.36.2	divā sāma samadadhāt
1.1.36.3	sāmnādityam
1.1.36.4	ādityena raśmīn
1.1.36.5	raśmibhir varṣam
1.1.36.6	varṣeṇauṣadhivanaspatīn
1.1.36.7	oṣadhivanaspatibhiḥ paśūn
1.1.36.8	paśubhiḥ karma
1.1.36.9	karmaṇā tapaḥ
1.1.36.10	tapasā satyam
1.1.36.11	satyena brahma
1.1.36.12	brahmaṇā brāhmaṇam
1.1.36.13	brāhmaṇena vratam
1.1.36.14	vratena vai brāhmaṇaḥ saṃśito bhavati
1.1.36.15	aśūnyo bhavaty avicchinno bhavaty avicchinno 'sya tantur avicchinnaṃ jīvanaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda yaś caivaṃ vidvān evam etaṃ sāvitryās tṛtīyaṃ pādaṃ vyācaṣṭe
1.1.37.1	tena ha vā evaṃ viduṣā brāhmaṇena brahmābhipannaṃ grasitaṃ parāmṛṣṭam
1.1.37.2	brahmaṇākāśam abhipannaṃ grasitaṃ parāmṛṣṭam
1.1.37.3	ākāśena vāyur abhipanno grasitaḥ parāmṛṣṭaḥ
1.1.37.4	vāyunā jyotir abhipannaṃ grasitaṃ parāmṛṣṭam
1.1.37.5	jyotiṣāpo 'bhipannā grasitāḥ parāmṛṣṭāḥ
1.1.37.6	adbhir bhūmir abhipannā grasitā parāmṛṣṭā
1.1.37.7	bhūmyānnam abhipannaṃ grasitaṃ parāmṛṣṭam
1.1.37.8	annena prāṇo 'bhipanno grasitaḥ parāmṛṣṭaḥ
1.1.37.9	prāṇena mano 'bhipannaṃ grasitaṃ parāmṛṣṭam
1.1.37.10	manasā vāg abhipannā grasitā parāmṛṣṭā
1.1.37.11	vācā vedā abhipannā grasitāḥ parāmṛṣṭāḥ
1.1.37.12	vedair yajño 'bhipanno grasitaḥ parāmṛṣṭaḥ
1.1.37.13	tāni ha vā etāni dvādaśa mahābhūtāny evaṃvidi pratiṣṭhitāni
1.1.37.14	teṣāṃ yajña eva parārdhyaḥ
1.1.38.1	taṃ ha smaitam evaṃ vidvāṃso manyante vidmainam iti yāthātathyam avidvāṃsaḥ
1.1.38.2	ayaṃ yajño vedeṣu pratiṣṭhitaḥ
1.1.38.3	vedā vāci pratiṣṭhitāḥ
1.1.38.4	vāṅ manasi pratiṣṭhitā
1.1.38.5	manaḥ prāṇe pratiṣṭhitam
1.1.38.6	prāṇo 'nne pratiṣṭhitaḥ
1.1.38.7	annaṃ bhūmau pratiṣṭhitam
1.1.38.8	bhūmir apsu pratiṣṭhitā
1.1.38.9	āpo jyotiṣi pratiṣṭhitāḥ
1.1.38.10	jyotir vāyau pratiṣṭhitam
1.1.38.11	vāyur ākāśe pratiṣṭhitaḥ
1.1.38.12	ākāśaṃ brahmaṇi pratiṣṭhitam
1.1.38.13	brahma brāhmaṇe brahmavidi pratiṣṭhitam
1.1.38.14	yo ha vā evaṃvit sa brahmavit
1.1.38.15	puṇyāṃ ca kīrtiṃ labhate surabhīṃś ca gandhān
1.1.38.16	so 'pahatapāpmā
1.1.38.17	anantāṃ śriyam aśnute ya evaṃ veda yaś caivaṃ vidvān evam etāṃ vedānāṃ mātaraṃ sāvitrīṃ saṃpadam upaniṣadam upāsta iti brāhmaṇam
1.1.39.1	āpo garbhaṃ janayantīr iti
1.1.39.2	apāṃ garbhaḥ puruṣaḥ
1.1.39.3	sa yajñaḥ
1.1.39.4	adbhir yajñaḥ praṇīyamānaḥ prāṅ tāyate
1.1.39.5	tasmād ācamanīyaṃ pūrvam āhārayati
1.1.39.6	sa yad ācāmati trir ācāmati
1.1.39.7	dviḥ pariśumbhati
1.1.39.8	āyur avaruhya pāpmānaṃ nirṇudati
1.1.39.9	upasādya yajuṣoddhṛtya mantrān prayujyāvasāya prācīḥ śākhāḥ saṃdhāya niraṅguṣṭhe pāṇāv amṛtam asy amṛtopastaraṇam asy amṛtāya tvopastṛṇāmīti pāṇāv udakam ānīya jīvā stheti sūktena trir ācāmati
1.1.39.10	sa yat pūrvam ācāmati sapta prāṇāṃs tān etenāsminn āpyāyayati
1.1.39.11	yā hy emā bāhyāḥ śarīrān mātrās tad yathaitad agniṃ vāyum ādityaṃ candramasam apaḥ paśūn anyāṃś ca prajās tān etenāsminn āpyāyayati
1.1.39.12	āpo 'mṛtam
1.1.39.13	sa yad dvitīyam ācāmati saptāpānāṃs tān etenāsminn āpyāyayati
1.1.39.14	yā hy emā bāhyāḥ śarīrān mātrās tad yathaitat paurṇamāsīm aṣṭakām amāvāsyāṃ śraddhāṃ dīkṣāṃ yajñaṃ dakṣiṇās tān etenāsminn āpyāyayati
1.1.39.15	āpo 'mṛtam
1.1.39.16	sa yat tṛtīyam ācāmati sapta vyānāṃs tān etenāsminn āpyāyayati
1.1.39.17	yā hy emā bāhyāḥ śarīrān mātrās tad yathaitat pṛthivīm antarikṣaṃ divam
1.1.39.18	nakṣatrāṇy ṛtūn ārtavān saṃvatsarāṃs tān etenāsminn āpyāyayati
1.1.39.19	āpo 'mṛtam
1.1.39.20	puruṣo brahma
1.1.39.21	athāprīṃgnigamo bhavati tasmād vai vidvān puruṣam idaṃ puṇḍarīkam iti
1.1.39.22	prāṇa eṣa sa puri śete saṃ puri śeta iti
1.1.39.23	puriśayaṃ santaṃ prāṇaṃ puruṣa ity ācakṣate parokṣeṇa
1.1.39.24	parokṣapriyā iva hi devā bhavanti pratyakṣadviṣaḥ
1.1.39.25	sa yat pūrvam ācāmati purastāddhomāṃs tenāsminn avarunddhe
1.1.39.26	sa yad dvitīyam ācāmaty ājyabhāgau tenāsminn avarunddhe
1.1.39.27	sa yat tṛtīyam ācāmati saṃsthitahomāṃs tenāsminn avarunddhe
1.1.39.28	sa yad dviḥ pariśumbhati tat samitsaṃbarhiḥ
1.1.39.29	sa yat sarvāṇi khāni sarvaṃ deham āpyāyayati yac cānyadātāraṃ mantrakāryaṃ yajñe skandati sarvaṃ tenāsminnavarunddhe
1.1.39.30	sa yad oṃpūrvān mantrān prayuṅkta ā sarvamedhād ete kratava eta evāsya sarveṣu lokeṣu sarveṣu deveṣu sarveṣu vedeṣu sarveṣu bhūteṣu sarveṣu sattveṣu kāmacāraḥ kāmavimocanaṃ bhavaty ardhe ca na pramīyate ya evaṃ veda
1.1.39.31	tad apy etad ṛcoktam āpo bhṛgvaṅgirorūpam āpo bhṛgvaṅgiromayaṃ sarvam āpomayaṃ bhūtaṃ sarvaṃ bhṛgvaṅgiromayam antaraite trayo vedā bhṛgūn aṅgiraso 'nugāḥ
1.1.39.32	apāṃ puṣpaṃ mūrtir ākāśaṃ pavitram uttamam iti
1.1.39.33	ācamyābhyukṣyātmānam anumantrayata indra jīveti brāhmaṇam
1.2.1.1	oṃ brahmacārīṣṇaṃś carati rodasī ubhe ity ācāryam āha
1.2.1.2	tasmin devāḥ saṃmanaso bhavantīti vāyum āha
1.2.1.3	sa sadya eti pūrvasmād uttaraṃ samudram ity ādityam āha
1.2.1.4	dīkṣito dīrghaśmaśruḥ
1.2.1.5	eṣa dīkṣita eṣa dīrghaśmaśrur eṣa evācāryasthāne tiṣṭhann ācārya iti stūyate
1.2.1.6	vaidyutasthāne tiṣṭhan vāyur iti stūyate dyausthāne tiṣṭhann āditya iti stūyate
1.2.1.7	tad apy etad ṛcoktaṃ brahmacārīṣṇan iti brāhmaṇam
1.2.2.1	jāyamāno ha vai brāhmaṇaḥ saptendriyāṇy abhijāyate brahmavarcasaṃ ca yaśaś ca svapnaṃ ca krodhaṃ ca ślāghāṃ ca rūpaṃ ca puṇyam eva gandhaṃ saptamam
1.2.2.2	tāni ha vā asyaitāni brahmacaryam upetyopakrāmanti
1.2.2.3	mṛgān asya brahmavarcasaṃ gacchati
1.2.2.4	ācāryaṃ yaśaḥ
1.2.2.5	ajagaraṃ svapnaḥ
1.2.2.6	varāhaṃ krodhaḥ
1.2.2.7	apaḥ ślāghā
1.2.2.8	kumārīṃ rūpam
1.2.2.9	oṣadhivanaspatīn puṇyo gandhaḥ
1.2.2.10	sa yan mṛgājināni vaste tena tad brahmavarcasam avarunddhe yad asya mṛgeṣu bhavati
1.2.2.11	sa ha snāto brahmavarcasī bhavati
1.2.2.12	sa yad aharahar ācāryāya karma karoti tena tad yaśo 'varunddhe yad asyācārye bhavati
1.2.2.13	sa ha snāto yaśasvī bhavati
1.2.2.14	sa yat suṣupsur nidrāṃ ninayati tena taṃ svapnam avarunddhe yo 'syājagare bhavati
1.2.2.15	taṃ ha snātaṃ svapantam āhuḥ svapitu mainaṃ bobudhatheti
1.2.2.16	sa yat kruddho vācā na kaṃcana hinasti puruṣātpuruṣāt pāpīyān iva manyamānas tena taṃ krodham avarunddhe yo 'sya varāhe bhavati
1.2.2.17	tasya ha snātasya krodhāḥ ślāghīyasaṃ viśante
1.2.2.18	athādbhiḥ ślāghamāno na snāyāt
1.2.2.19	tena tāṃ ślāghām avarunddhe yāsyāpsu bhavati
1.2.2.20	sa ha snātaḥ ślāghīyo 'nyebhyaḥ ślāghyate
1.2.2.21	athaitad brahmacāriṇo rūpaṃ yat kumāryāḥ
1.2.2.22	tāṃ nagnāṃ nodīkṣeta
1.2.2.23	iti veti vā mukhaṃ viparidhāpayet
1.2.2.24	tena tad rūpam avarunddhe yad asya kumāryāṃ bhavati
1.2.2.25	taṃ ha snātaṃ kumārīm iva nirīkṣante
1.2.2.26	athaitad brahmacāriṇaḥ puṇyo gandho ya oṣadhivanaspatīnāṃ tāsāṃ puṇyaṃ gandhaṃ pracchidya nopajighret
1.2.2.27	tena taṃ puṇyaṃ gandham avarunddhe yo 'syauṣadhivanaspatiṣu bhavati
1.2.2.28	sa ha snātaḥ puṇyagandhir bhavati
1.2.3.1	sa vā eṣa upayaṃś caturdhopaity agniṃ pādenācāryaṃ pādena grāmaṃ pādena mṛtyuṃ pādena
1.2.3.2	sa yad aharahaḥ samidha āhṛtya sāyaṃ prātar agniṃ paricaret tena taṃ pādam avarunddhe yo 'syāgnau bhavati
1.2.3.3	sa yad aharahar ācāryāya karma karoti tena taṃ pādam avarunddhe yo 'syācārye bhavati
1.2.3.4	sa yad aharahar grāmaṃ praviśya bhikṣām eva parīpsati na maithunaṃ tena taṃ pādam avarunddhe yo 'sya grāme bhavati
1.2.3.5	sa yat kruddho vācā na kaṃcana hinasti puruṣātpuruṣāt pāpīyān iva manyamānas tena taṃ pādam avarunddhe yo 'sya mṛtyau bhavati
1.2.4.1	pañca ha vā ete brahmacāriṇy agnayo dhīyante
1.2.4.2	dvau pṛthagghastayor mukhe hṛdaya upastha eva pañcamaḥ
1.2.4.3	sa yad dakṣiṇena pāṇinā striyaṃ na spṛśati tenāharahar yājināṃ lokam avarunddhe
1.2.4.4	yat savyena tena pravrājinām
1.2.4.5	yan mukhena tenāgnipraskandinām
1.2.4.6	yaddhṛdayena tena śūrāṇām
1.2.4.7	yad upasthena tena gṛhamedhinām
1.2.4.8	taiś cet striyaṃ parāharaty anagnir iva śiṣyate
1.2.4.9	sa yad aharahar ācāryāya kule 'nutiṣṭhate so 'nuṣṭhāya brūyād dharma gupto mā gopāyeti
1.2.4.10	dharmo hainaṃ gupto gopāyati
1.2.4.11	tasya ha prajā śvaḥ śvaḥ śreyasī śreyasīha bhavati
1.2.4.12	dhāyyaiva pratidhīyate
1.2.4.13	svarge loke pitṝn nidadhāti
1.2.4.14	tāntavaṃ na vasīta
1.2.4.15	yas tāntavaṃ vaste kṣatraṃ vardhate na brahma
1.2.4.16	tasmāt tāntavaṃ na vasīta brahma vardhatāṃ mā kṣatram iti
1.2.4.17	nopary āsīta
1.2.4.18	yad upary āste prāṇam eva tadātmano 'dharaṃ kurute yad vāto vahati
1.2.4.19	adha evāsītādhaḥ śayītādhas tiṣṭhed adho vrajet
1.2.4.20	evaṃ ha sma vai tat pūrve brāhmaṇā brahmacaryaṃ caranti
1.2.4.21	taṃ ha sma tatputraṃ bhrātaraṃ vopatāpinam āhur upanayetainam iti
1.2.4.22	ā samiddhārāt svar eṣyanto 'nnam adyāt
1.2.4.23	athāha jaghanam āhuḥ snāpayetainam ity ā samiddhārāt
1.2.4.24	na hy etāni vratāni bhavanti
1.2.4.25	taṃ cec chayānam ācāryo 'bhivadet sa pratisaṃhāya pratiśṛṇuyāt
1.2.4.26	taṃ cec chayānam utthāya taṃ ced utthitam abhiprakramya taṃ ced abhiprakrāntam abhipalāyamānam
1.2.4.27	evaṃ ha sma vai tat pūrve brāhmaṇā brahmacaryaṃ caranti
1.2.4.28	teṣāṃ ha sma vaiṣā puṇyā kīrtir gacchaty ā ha vā ayaṃ so 'dya gamiṣyatīti
1.2.5.1	janamejayo ha vai pārīkṣito mṛgayāṃ cariṣyan haṃsābhyām asiṣyann upāvatastha iti
1.2.5.2	tāv ūcatur janamejayaṃ pārīkṣitam abhyājagāma
1.2.5.3	sa hovāca
1.2.5.4	namo vāṃ bhagavantau kau nu bhagavantāv iti
1.2.5.5	tāv ūcatur dakṣiṇāgniś cāhavanīyaś ceti
1.2.5.6	sa hovāca namo vāṃ bhagavantau tadākīyatām iti
1.2.5.7	ihopārāmam iti
1.2.5.8	api kila devā na ramante na hi devā na ramante
1.2.5.9	api caikopārāmād devā ārāmam upasaṃkrāmantīti
1.2.5.10	sa hovāca namo vāṃ bhagavantau kiṃ puṇyam iti
1.2.5.11	brahmacaryam iti
1.2.5.12	kiṃ laukyam iti
1.2.5.13	brahmacaryam eveti
1.2.5.14	tat ko veda iti
1.2.5.15	dantāvalo dhaumraḥ
1.2.5.16	atha khalu dantāvalo dhaumro yāvati tāvati kāle pārīkṣitaṃ janamejayam abhyājagāma
1.2.5.17	tasmā utthāya svayam eva viṣṭaraṃ nidadhau
1.2.5.18	tam upasaṃgṛhya papracchādhīhi bho kiṃ puṇyam iti
1.2.5.19	brahmacaryam iti
1.2.5.20	kiṃ laukyam iti
1.2.5.21	brahmacaryam eveti
1.2.5.22	tasmā etat provācāṣṭācatvāriṃśadvarṣaṃ sarvavedabrahmacaryam
1.2.5.23	tac caturdhā vedeṣu vyuhya dvādaśavarṣaṃ brahmacaryaṃ dvādaśavarṣāṇy avarārdham
1.2.5.24	api snāyaṃś cared yathāśakty aparam
1.2.5.25	tasmā uhasyṛṣabhau sahasraṃ dadau
1.2.5.26	apy apakīrtitam ācāryo brahmacārīty eka āhur ākāśam adhidaivatam
1.2.5.27	athādhyātmaṃ brāhmaṇo vratavāṃś caraṇavān brahmacārī
1.2.6.1	brahma ha vai prajā mṛtyave samprāyacchat
1.2.6.2	brahmacāriṇam eva na sampradadau
1.2.6.3	sa hovācāśyām asminn iti
1.2.6.4	kim iti
1.2.6.5	yāṃ rātrīṃ samidham anāhṛtya vaset tām āyuṣo 'varundhīyeti
1.2.6.6	tasmād brahmacāry aharahaḥ samidha āhṛtya sāyaṃ prātar agniṃ paricaret
1.2.6.7	nopary upasādayed atha pratiṣṭhāpayet
1.2.6.8	yad upary upasādayej jīmūtavarṣī tad ahaḥ parjanyo bhavati
1.2.6.9	te devā abruvan brāhmaṇo vā ayaṃ brahmacaryaṃ cariṣyati
1.2.6.10	brūtāsmai bhikṣā iti gṛhapatir brūta bahucārī gṛhapatnyā iti
1.2.6.11	kim asyā vṛñjītādadatyā iti
1.2.6.12	iṣṭāpūrtasukṛtadraviṇam avarundhyād iti
1.2.6.13	tasmād brahmacāriṇe 'harahar bhikṣāṃ dadyād gṛhiṇī mā māyam iṣṭāpūrtasukṛtadraviṇam avarundhyād iti
1.2.6.14	saptamīṃ nātinayet saptamīm atinayan na brahmacārī bhavati
1.2.6.15	samidbhaikṣe saptarātram acaritavān brahmacārī punarupaneyo bhavati
1.2.7.1	nopariśāyī syān na gāyano na nartano na saraṇo na niṣṭhīvet
1.2.7.2	yad upariśāyī bhavaty abhīkṣṇaṃ nivāsā jāyante
1.2.7.3	yad gāyano bhavaty abhīkṣṇaśa ākrandān dhāvante
1.2.7.4	yan nartano bhavaty abhīkṣṇaśaḥ pretān nirharante
1.2.7.5	yat saraṇo bhavaty abhīkṣṇaśaḥ prajāḥ saṃviśante
1.2.7.6	yan niṣṭhīvati madhya eva tadātmano niṣṭhīvati
1.2.7.7	sa cen niṣṭhīved divo nu mām yad atrāpi madhor ahaṃ yad atrāpi rasasya me ity ātmānam anumantrayate
1.2.7.8	yad atrāpi madhor ahaṃ niraṣṭhaviṣam asmṛtam agniś ca tat savitā ca punar me jaṭhare dhattāṃ yad atrāpi rasasya me parāpapātāsmṛtaṃ tad ihopahvayāmahe tan ma āpyāyatāṃ punar iti
1.2.7.9	na śmaśānam ātiṣṭhet
1.2.7.10	sa ced abhitiṣṭhed udakaṃ haste kṛtvā yadīdam ṛtukāmyety abhimantrya japant samprokṣya parikrāmet
1.2.7.11	samayāyoparivrajet
1.2.7.12	yadīdam ṛtukāmyāghaṃ ripram upeyima andhaḥ śloṇa iva hīyatāṃ mā no 'nvāgād aghaṃ yata iti
1.2.7.13	atha haitad devānāṃ pariṣūtaṃ yad brahmacārī
1.2.7.14	tad apy etad ṛcoktaṃ devānām etat pariṣūtam anabhyārūḍhaṃ carati rocamānaṃ tasmin sarve paśavas tatra yajñās tasminn annaṃ saha devatābhir iti brāhmaṇam
1.2.8.1	prāṇāpānau janayann iti śaṅkhasya mukhe maharṣer vasiṣṭhasya putra etāṃ vācaṃ sasṛje śītoṣṇāv ihotsau prādurbhaveyātām iti
1.2.8.2	tathā tac chaśvad anuvartate
1.2.8.3	atha khalu vipāṇmadhye vasiṣṭhaśilā nāma prathama āśramaḥ
1.2.8.4	dvitīyaḥ kṛṣṇaśilāḥ
1.2.8.5	tasmin vasiṣṭhaḥ samatapat
1.2.8.6	viśvāmitrajamadagnī jāmadagne tapataḥ
1.2.8.7	gautamabharadvājau siṃhau prabhave tapataḥ
1.2.8.8	guṃgur guṃguvāse tapati
1.2.8.9	ṛṣir ṛṣidroṇe 'bhyatapat
1.2.8.10	agastyo 'gastyatīrthe tapati
1.2.8.11	divy atrir ha tapati
1.2.8.12	svayambhūḥ kaśyapaḥ kaśyapatuṅge 'bhyatapat
1.2.8.13	ulavṛkarkṣutarakṣuḥ śvā varāhacilvaṭibabrukāḥ sarpadaṃṣṭranaḥ saṃhanukṛṇvānāḥ kaśyapatuṅgadarśanāt saraṇavāṭāt siddhir bhavati
1.2.8.14	brāhmyaṃ varṣasahasram ṛṣivane brahmacāryekapādenātiṣṭhati
1.2.8.15	dvitīyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ mūrdhany evāmṛtasya dhārām ādhārayat
1.2.8.16	brāhmāṇyaṣṭācatvāriṃśadvarṣasahasrāṇi salilasya pṛṣṭhe śivo 'bhyatapat
1.2.8.17	tasmāt taptāt tapaso bhūya evābhyatapat
1.2.8.18	tad apy etā ṛco 'bhivadanti prāṇāpānau janayann iti brāhmaṇam
1.2.9.1	ekapād dvipada iti
1.2.9.2	vāyur ekapāt
1.2.9.3	tasyākāśaṃ pādaḥ
1.2.9.4	candramā dvipāt
1.2.9.5	tasya pūrvapakṣāparapakṣau pādau
1.2.9.6	ādityas tripāt
1.2.9.7	tasyeme lokāḥ pādāḥ
1.2.9.8	agniḥ ṣaṭpādaḥ
1.2.9.9	tasya pṛthivy antarikṣaṃ dyaur āpa oṣadhivanaspataya imāni bhūtāni pādāḥ
1.2.9.10	teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ vedā gatir ātmā pratiṣṭhitāś catasro brahmaṇaḥ śākhāḥ
1.2.9.11	atho āhuḥ ṣaḍ iti mūrtir ākāśaś ceti
1.2.9.12	ṛcā mūrtiḥ
1.2.9.13	yājuṣī gatiḥ
1.2.9.14	sāmamayaṃ tejaḥ
1.2.9.15	bhṛgvaṅgirasā māyā
1.2.9.16	etad brahmaiva yajñaś catuṣpād dviḥ saṃsthita iti
1.2.9.17	tasya bhṛgvaṅgirasaḥ saṃsthe
1.2.9.18	atho āhur ekasaṃsthita iti
1.2.9.19	yaddhotarcāṃ maṇḍalaiḥ karoti pṛthivīṃ tenāpyāyayati
1.2.9.20	etasyāṃ hy agniś carati
1.2.9.21	tad apy etad ṛcoktam agnivāsāḥ pṛthivy asitajñūr iti
1.2.9.22	yad adhvaryur yajuṣā karoty antarikṣaṃ tenāpyāyayati
1.2.9.23	tasmin vāyur na niviśate katamac ca nāhar iti
1.2.9.24	tad apy etad ṛcoktam antarikṣe pathibhir hrīyamāṇo na niviśate katamac ca nāhaḥ apāṃ yoniḥ prathamajā ṛtasya kva svij jātaḥ kuta ābabhūveti
1.2.9.25	yad udgātā sāmnā karoti divaṃ tenāpyāyayati
1.2.9.26	tatra hy ādityaḥ śukraś carati
1.2.9.27	tad apy etad ṛcoktam uccā patantam aruṇaṃ suparṇam iti
1.2.9.28	yad brahmarcāṃ kāṇḍaiḥ karoty apas tenāpyāyayati
1.2.9.29	candramā hy apsu carati
1.2.9.30	tad apy etad ṛcoktaṃ candramā apsv antar iti tāsām oṣadhivanaspatayaḥ kāṇḍāni
1.2.9.31	tato mūlakāṇḍaparṇapuṣpaphalapraroharasagandhair yajño vartate
1.2.9.32	adbhiḥ karṇāṇi pravartante
1.2.9.33	adbhiḥ somo 'bhiṣūyate
1.2.9.34	tad yad brahmāṇāṃ karṇāṇi karmaṇy āmantrayaty apas tenānujānāti
1.2.9.35	eṣo hy asya bhāgaḥ
1.2.9.36	tad yathā bhokṣyamāṇaḥ
1.2.9.37	apa eva prathamam ācāmayed apa upariṣṭād evaṃ yajño 'dbhir eva pravartate
1.2.9.38	apsu saṃsthāpyate tasmād brahmā purastāddhomasaṃsthitahomair yajño vartate
1.2.9.39	antarā hi purastāddhomasaṃsthitahomair yajñaṃ parigṛhṇāti
1.2.9.40	antarā hi bhṛgvaṅgiraso vedān āduhya bhṛgvaṅgirasaḥ somapānaṃ manyante
1.2.9.41	somātmako hy ayaṃ veda
1.2.9.42	tad apy etad ṛcoktaṃ somaṃ manyate papivān iti
1.2.9.43	tad yathemāṃ pṛthivīm udīrṇāṃ jyotiṣā dhūmāyamānāṃ varṣaṃ śamayati
1.2.9.44	evaṃ brahmā bhṛgvaṅgirobhir vyāhṛtibhir yajñasya viriṣṭaṃ śamayati
1.2.9.45	agnir ādityāya śamayati
1.2.9.46	ete 'ṅgirasaḥ
1.2.9.47	eta idaṃ sarvaṃ samāpnuvanti
1.2.9.48	vāyur āpaś candramā ity ete bhṛgavaḥ
1.2.9.49	eta idaṃ sarvaṃ samāpyāyayanti
1.2.9.50	ekam eva saṃsthaṃ bhavatīti brāhmaṇam
1.2.10.1	vicārī ha vai kābandhiḥ kabandhasyātharvaṇasya putro medhāvī mīmāṃsako 'nūcāna āsa
1.2.10.2	sa ha svenātimānena mānuṣaṃ vittaṃ neyāya
1.2.10.3	taṃ mātovāca
1.2.10.4	ta evaitad annam avocaṃs ta ima eṣu kurupañcāleṣv aṅgamagadheṣu kāśikauśaleṣu śālvamatsyeṣu savaśośīnareṣūdīcyeṣv annam adantīti
1.2.10.5	atha vayaṃ tavaivātimānenānādyāḥ smaḥ
1.2.10.6	vatsa vāhanam anviccheti
1.2.10.7	sa māndhātur yauvanāśvasya sārvabhaumasya rājñaḥ somaṃ prasūtam ājagāma
1.2.10.8	sa sado 'nupraviśyartvijaś ca yajamānaṃ cāmantrayāmāsa
1.2.10.9	tad yāḥ prācyo nadyo vahanti yāś ca dakṣiṇācyo yāś ca pratīcyo yāś codīcyas tāḥ sarvāḥ pṛthaṅnāmadheyā ity ācakṣate
1.2.10.10	tāsāṃ samudram abhipadyamānānāṃ chidyate nāmadheyaṃ samudra ity ācakṣate
1.2.10.11	evam ime sarve vedā nirmitāḥ sakalpāḥ sarahasyāḥ sabrāhmaṇāḥ sopaniṣatkāḥ setihāsāḥ sānvākhyānāḥ sapurāṇāḥ sasvarāḥ sasaṃskārāḥ saniruktāḥ sānuśāsanāḥ sānumārjanāḥ savākovākyāḥ
1.2.10.12	teṣāṃ yajñam abhipadyamānānāṃ chidyate nāmadheyaṃ yajña ity evācakṣate
1.2.11.1	bhūmer ha vā etad vicchinnaṃ devayajanaṃ yad aprākpravaṇaṃ yad anudakpravaṇaṃ yatkṛtrimaṃ yat samaviṣamam
1.2.11.2	idaṃ ha tv eva devayajanaṃ yat samaṃ samūlam avidagdhaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ prāgudakpravaṇaṃ samaṃ samāstīrṇam iva bhavati yatra brāhmaṇasya brāhmaṇatāṃ vidyād brahmā brahmatvaṃ karotīti
1.2.11.3	voce chandas tan na vindāmo yenottaram emahīti
1.2.11.4	tān ha papraccha kiṃ vidvān hotā hautraṃ karoti kiṃ vidvān adhvaryur ādhvaryavaṃ karoti kiṃ vidvān udgātaudgātraṃ karoti kiṃ vidvān brahmā brahmatvaṃ karotīti
1.2.11.5	voce chandas tan na vindāmo yenottaram emahīti
1.2.11.6	te brūmo vāg eva hotā hautraṃ karoti
1.2.11.7	vāco hi stomāś ca vaṣaṭkārāś cābhisaṃpadyante
1.2.11.8	te brūmo vāg eva hotā vāg brahma vāg deva iti
1.2.11.9	prāṇāpānābhyām evādhvaryur ādhvaryavaṃ karoti
1.2.11.10	prāṇapraṇītāni ha bhūtāni prāṇapraṇītāḥ praṇītāḥ
1.2.11.11	te brūmaḥ prāṇāpānāv evādhvaryuḥ prāṇāpānau brahma prāṇāpānau deva iti
1.2.11.12	cakṣuṣaivodgātaudgātraṃ karoti
1.2.11.13	cakṣuṣā hīmāni bhūtāni paśyanti
1.2.11.14	atho cakṣur evodgātā cakṣur brahma cakṣur deva iti
1.2.11.15	manasaiva brahmā brahmatvaṃ karoti
1.2.11.16	manasā hi tiryak ca diśa ūrdhvaṃ yac ca kiṃca manasaiva karoti tad brahma
1.2.11.17	te brūmo mana eva brahmā mano brahma mano deva iti
1.2.12.1	tad yathā ha vā idaṃ yajamānaś ca yājayitāraś ca divaṃ brūyuḥ pṛthivīti pṛthivīṃ vā dyaur iti brūyus tad anyo nānujānāty etām evaṃ nānujānāti yad etad brūyāt
1.2.12.2	atha nu katham iti
1.2.12.3	hotety eva hotāraṃ brūyād vāg iti vācaṃ brahmeti brahma deva iti devam adhvaryur ity evādhvaryuṃ brūyāt prāṇāpānāv iti prāṇāpānau brahmeti brahma deva iti devam udgātety evodgātāraṃ brūyāc cakṣur iti cakṣur brahmeti brahma deva iti devaṃ brahmety eva brahmāṇaṃ brūyān mana iti mano brahmeti brahma deva iti devam
1.2.13.1	nānāpravacanāni ha vā etāni bhūtāni bhavanti
1.2.13.2	ye caivāsomapaṃ yājayanti ye ca surāpaṃ ye ca brāhmaṇaṃ vicchinnaṃ somayājinaṃ taṃ prātaḥ samitpāṇaya upodeyur upāyāmo bhavantam iti

1.2.15.4	tata ādityā ajāyanta
1.2.15.5	ya eṣa odanaḥ pacyata ārambhaṇam evaitat kriyata ākramaṇam eva

1.2.16.1	prajāpatir atharvā devaḥ sa tapas taptvaitaṃ cātuḥprāśyaṃ brahmaudanaṃ niramimīta caturlokaṃ caturdevaṃ caturvedaṃ caturhautram iti
1.2.16.2	catvāro vā ime lokāḥ pṛthivy antarikṣaṃ dyaur āpa iti
1.2.16.3	catvāro vā ime devā agnir vāyur ādityaś candramāḥ
1.2.16.4	catvāro vā ime vedā ṛgvedo yajurvedaḥ sāmavedo brahmaveda iti
1.2.16.5	catasro vā imā hotrā hautram ādhvaryavam audgātraṃ brahmatvam iti
1.2.16.6	tad apy etad ṛcoktaṃ catvāri śṛṅgā trayo asya pādā dve śīrṣe sapta hastāso asya tridhā baddho vṛṣabho roravīti maho devo martyāṁ āviveśeti
1.2.16.7	catvāri śṛṅgeti vedā vā eta uktāḥ

1.2.16.13	maho devo martyāṁ āviveśety eṣa ha vai mahān devo yad yajñaḥ
1.2.16.14	eṣa martyāṁ āviveśa

1.2.18.1	prajāpatir vedān uvācāgnīn ādadhīyeti

1.2.18.5	tatheti
1.2.18.6	tam ṛgveda etyovācāham aśvaṃ śameyam iti

1.2.19.1	devāś ca ha vā asurāś cāspardhanta
1.2.19.2	te devā indram abruvann imaṃ nas tāvad yajñaṃ gopāya yāvad asuraiḥ saṃyatāmahā iti
1.2.19.3	sa vai nas tena rūpeṇa gopāya yena no rūpeṇa bhūyiṣṭhaṃ chādayasi yena śakṣyasi goptum iti
1.2.19.4	sa ṛgvedo bhūtvā purastāt parītyopātiṣṭhat
1.2.19.5	taṃ devā abruvann anyat tad rūpaṃ kuruṣva naitena no rūpeṇa bhūyiṣṭhaṃ chādayasi naitena śakṣyasi goptum iti
1.2.19.6	sa yajurvedo bhūtvā paścāt parītyopātiṣṭhat
1.2.19.7	taṃ devā abruvann anyat tad rūpaṃ kuruṣva naitena no rūpeṇa bhūyiṣṭhaṃ chādayasi naitena śakṣyasi goptum iti
1.2.19.8	sa sāmavedo bhūtvottarataḥ parītyopātiṣṭhat
1.2.19.9	taṃ devā abruvann anyad eva tad rūpaṃ kuruṣva naitena no rūpeṇa bhūyiṣṭhaṃ chādayasi naitena śakṣyasi goptum iti
1.2.19.10	sa indra uṣṇīṣī brahmavedo bhūtvā dakṣiṇataḥ parītyopātiṣṭhat
1.2.19.11	taṃ devā abruvann etat tad rūpaṃ kuruṣvaitena no rūpeṇa bhūyiṣṭhaṃ chādayasy etena śakṣyasi goptum iti
1.2.19.12	tad yad indra uṣṇīṣī brahmavedo bhūtvā dakṣiṇataḥ parītyopātiṣṭhat tad brahmābhavat
1.2.19.13	tad brahmaṇo brahmatvam

1.2.19.17	tat sadasyasya sadasyatvam
1.2.19.18	baler ha vā etad balam upajāyate yat sadasye
1.2.19.19	āmayato vai vrajasya bahulataraṃ vrajaṃ vidanti
1.2.19.20	ghorā vā eṣā dig dakṣiṇā śāntā itarāḥ

1.2.19.23	taṃ devā abruvan varaṃ vṛṇīṣveti
1.2.19.24	vṛṇā iti
1.2.19.25	sa varam avṛṇīta
1.2.19.26	asyām eva māṃ hotrāyām indrabhūtaṃ punanta stuvantaḥ śaṃsantas tiṣṭheyur iti
1.2.19.27	taṃ tasyām eva hotrāyām indrabhūtaṃ punanta stuvantaḥ śaṃsanto 'tiṣṭhan
1.2.19.28	taṃ yat tasyām eva hotrāyām indrabhūtaṃ punanta stuvantaḥ śaṃsanto 'tiṣṭhaṃs tad brāhmaṇācchaṃsy abhavat

1.2.19.30	saiṣaindrī hotrā yad brāhmaṇācchaṃsīyā
1.2.19.31	dvitīyaṃ varaṃ vṛṇīṣveti
1.2.19.32	vṛṇā iti
1.2.19.33	sa varam avṛṇīta
1.2.19.34	asyām eva māṃ hotrāyāṃ vāyubhūtaṃ punanta stuvantaḥ śaṃsantas tiṣṭheyur iti

1.2.20.1	brāhmaṇo ha vā imam agniṃ vaiśvānaraṃ babhāra
1.2.20.2	so 'yam agnir vaiśvānaro brāhmaṇena bhriyamāṇa imāṃl lokāñ janayate
1.2.20.3	athāyam īkṣate 'gnir jātavedā brāhmaṇadvitīyo ha vā ayam idam agnir vaiśvānaro jvalati
1.2.20.4	hantāhaṃ yan mayi teja indriyaṃ vīryaṃ tad darśayāmy uta vai mā bibhṛyād iti

1.2.22.1	atharvāṇaś ca ha vā aṅgirasaś ca bhṛgucakṣuṣī tad brahmābhivyapaśyan
1.2.22.2	tadajānan vayaṃ vā idaṃ sarvaṃ yad bhṛgvaṅgirasa iti
1.2.22.3	te devā brāhmyaṃ havir yat sāṃtapane 'gnāv ajuhavuḥ
1.2.22.4	etad vai brāhmyaṃ havir yat sāṃtapane 'gnau hūyate
1.2.22.5	eṣa ha vai sāṃtapano 'gnir yad brāhmaṇaḥ
1.2.22.6	tasyorjayorjāṃ devā abhajanta sumanasa eva svadhāṃ pitaraḥ śraddhayā svargaṃ lokaṃ brāhmaṇāḥ
1.2.22.7	tena sunvanty ṛṣayo 'ntata striyaḥ kevala ātmany avārundhata bāhyā ubhayena sunvanti
1.2.22.8	yad vai yajñe brāhmyaṃ havir na nirupyetānṛjavaḥ prājāpatyahaviṣo manuṣyā jāyeran
1.2.22.9	asau yāṃllokāñchṛṇviti pitā hy eṣa āhavanīyasya gārhapatyasya dakṣiṇāgner yo 'gnihotraṃ juhotīti
1.2.22.10	devāḥ priye dhāmani madanti
1.2.22.11	teṣām eṣo 'gniḥ sāṃtapanaḥ śreṣṭho bhavati
1.2.22.12	etasya vāci tṛptāyām agnis tṛpyati
1.2.22.13	prāṇe tṛpte vāyus tṛpyati
1.2.22.14	cakṣuṣi tṛpta ādityas tṛpyati
1.2.22.15	manasi tṛpte candramās tṛpyati
1.2.22.16	śrotre tṛpte diśaś cāntardeśāś ca tṛpyanti
1.2.22.17	sneheṣu tṛpteṣv āpas tṛpyanti
1.2.22.18	lomeṣu tṛpteṣv oṣadhivanaspatayas tṛpyanti
1.2.22.19	śarīre tṛpte pṛthivī tṛpyati
1.2.22.20	evam eṣo 'gniḥ sāṃtapanaḥ śreṣṭhas tṛptaḥ sarvāṃs tṛptāṃs tarpayatīti brāhmaṇam
1.2.23.1	sāṃtapanā idaṃ havir iti
1.2.23.2	eṣa ha vai sāṃtapano 'gnir yad brāhmaṇo yasya garbhādhānapuṃsavanasīmantonnayanajātakarmanāmakaraṇaniṣkramaṇānnaprāśanagodānacūḍākaraṇopanayanāplavanāgnihotravratacaryādīni kṛtāni bhavanti sa sāṃtapanaḥ
1.2.23.3	atha yo 'yamanagnikaḥ sa kumbhe loṣṭaḥ
1.2.23.4	tad yathā kumbhe loṣṭaḥ prakṣipto naiva śaucārthāya kalpate naiva śasyaṃ nirvartayaty evam evāyaṃ brāhmaṇo 'nagnikas tasya brāhmaṇasyānagnikasya naiva daivaṃ dadyān na pitryaṃ na cāsya svādhyāyāśiṣo na yajñāśiṣaḥ svargaṃgamā bhavanti
1.2.23.5	tad apy etad ṛcoktam agniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmahe hotāraṃ viśvavedasam asya yajñasya sukratum iti brāhmaṇam
1.2.24.1	atha ha prajāpatiḥ somena yakṣyamāṇo vedān uvāca kaṃ vo hotāraṃ vṛṇīya kam adhvaryuṃ kam udgātāraṃ kaṃ brāhmaṇam iti / ta ūcur ṛgvidam eva hotāraṃ vṛṇīṣva yajurvidam adhvaryuṃ sāmavidam udgātāram atharvāṅgirovidaṃ brāhmaṇam
1.2.24.2	tathā hāsya yajñaś caturṣu lokeṣu caturṣu deveṣu caturṣu vedeṣu catasṛṣu hotrāsu catuṣpād yajñaḥ pratitiṣṭhati / pratitiṣṭhati prajayā paśubhir ya evaṃ veda
1.2.24.3	tasmād ṛgvidam eva hotāraṃ vṛṇīṣva sa hi hautraṃ veda / agnir vai hotā
1.2.24.4	pṛthivī vā ṛcām āyatanam / agnir devatā gāyatraṃ chando bhūr iti śukram
1.2.24.5	tasmāt tam eva hotāraṃ vṛṇīṣvety etasya lokasya jitaye / etasya lokasya vijitaye
1.2.24.6	etasya lokasya saṃjitaye / etasya lokasyāvaruddhaye
1.2.24.7	etasya lokasya vivṛddhaye / etasya lokasya samṛddhaye
1.2.24.8	etasya lokasyodāttaye / etasya lokasya vyāptaye
1.2.24.9	etasya lokasya paryāptaye / etasya lokasya samāptaye
1.2.24.10	atha cen naivaṃvidaṃ hotāraṃ vṛṇute purastād evaiṣāṃ yajño ricyate / yajurvidam evādhvaryuṃ vṛṇīṣva sa hy ādhvaryavaṃ veda
1.2.24.11	vāyur vā adhvaryuḥ / antarikṣaṃ vai yajuṣām āyatanam
1.2.24.12	vāyur devatā traiṣṭubhaṃ chando bhuva iti śukram / tasmāt tam evādhvaryuṃ vṛṇīṣvety etasya lokasyety eva
1.2.24.13	atha cen naivaṃvidam adhvaryuṃ vṛṇute paścād evaiṣāṃ yajño ricyate / sāmavidam evodgātāraṃ vṛṇīṣva
1.2.24.14	sa hy audgātraṃ veda / ādityo vā udgātā
1.2.24.15	dyaur vai sāmnām āyatanam / ādityo devatā jāgataṃ chandaḥ svar iti śukram
1.2.24.16	tasmāt tam evodgātāraṃ vṛṇīṣvety etasya lokasyety eva / atha cen naivaṃvidam udgātāraṃ vṛṇuta uttarata evaiṣāṃ yajño ricyate
1.2.24.17	atharvāṅgirovidam eva brahmāṇaṃ vṛṇīṣva / sa hi brahmatvaṃ veda
1.2.24.18	candramā vai brahmā / āpo vai bhṛgvaṅgirasām āyatanam
1.2.24.19	candramā devatā vaidyutaś coṣṇikkākubhe chandasī om ity atharvaṇāṃ śukraṃ janad ity aṅgirasām / tasmāt tam eva brahmāṇaṃ vṛṇīṣvety etasya lokasya jitaye
1.2.24.20	etasya lokasya vijitaye / etasya lokasya saṃjitaye
1.2.24.21	etasya lokasyāvaruddhaye / etasya lokasya vivṛddhaye
1.2.24.22	etasya lokasya samṛddhaye / etasya lokasyodāttaye
1.2.24.23	etasya lokasya vyāptaye / etasya lokasya paryāptaye
1.2.24.24	etasya lokasya samāptaye / atha cen naivaṃvidaṃ brahmāṇaṃ vṛṇute dakṣiṇata evaiṣāṃ yajño ricyate dakṣiṇata evaiṣāṃ yajño ricyate
1.3.1.1	oṃ dakṣiṇāpravaṇā bhūmir dakṣiṇata āpo vahanti
1.3.1.2	tasmād yajñās tadbhūmer unnatataram iva bhavati yatra bhṛgvaṅgiraso viṣṭhāḥ
1.3.1.3	tad yathāpa imāṃllokān abhivahanty evam eva bhṛgvaṅgirasaḥ sarvān devān abhivahanti
1.3.1.4	evam evaiṣā vyāhṛtiḥ sarvān vedān abhivahaty om iti harcām om iti yajuṣām om iti sāmnām om iti sarvasyāhābhivādaḥ
1.3.1.5	taṃ ha smaitad uttaraṃ yajñe vidvāṃsaḥ kurvanti
1.3.1.6	devā brahmāṇa āgacchatāgacchateti
1.3.1.7	ete vai devā brahmāṇo yad bhṛgvaṅgirasaḥ
1.3.1.8	tān evaitad gṛṇānās tān vṛṇānā hvayanto manyante
1.3.1.9	nānyo 'bhṛgvaṅgirovido vṛto yajñam āgacchet
1.3.1.10	yajñasya tejasā teja āpnoty ūrjayorjāṃ yaśasā yaśaḥ
1.3.1.11	nānyo 'bhṛgvaṅgirovido vṛto yajñam āgacchen ned yajñaṃ parimuṣṇīyād iti
1.3.1.12	tad yathā pūrvaṃ vatso 'dhītya gāṃ dhayed evaṃ brahmā bhṛgvaṅgirovid vṛto yajñam āgacchen ned yajñaṃ parimuṣṇīyād iti
1.3.1.13	tad yathā gaur vāśvo vāśvataro vaikapād dvipāt tripād iti syāt kim abhivahet kim abhyaśnuyād iti
1.3.1.14	tasmād ṛgvidam eva hotāraṃ vṛṇīṣva yajurvidam adhvaryuṃ sāmavidam udgātāram atharvāṅgirovidaṃ brahmāṇam
1.3.1.15	tathā hāsya yajñaś caturṣu lokeṣu caturṣu deveṣu vedeṣu catasṛṣu hotrāsu catuṣpād yajñaḥ pratitiṣṭhati
1.3.1.16	pratitiṣṭhati prajayā paśubhir ya evaṃ veda yaś caivam ṛtvijām ārtvijyaṃ veda yaś ca yajñe yajanīyaṃ vedeti brāhmaṇam
1.3.2.1	prajāpatir yajñam atanuta
1.3.2.2	sa ṛcaiva hautram akarod yajuṣādhvaryavaṃ sāmnaudgātram atharvāṅgirobhir brahmatvam
1.3.2.3	taṃ vā etaṃ mahāvādyaṃ kurute yad ṛcaiva hautram akarod yajuṣādhvaryavaṃ sāmnaudgātram atharvāṅgirobhir brahmatvam
1.3.2.4	sa vā eṣa tribhir vedair yajñasyānyataraḥ pakṣaḥ saṃskriyate
1.3.2.5	manasaiva brahmā yajñasyānyataraṃ pakṣaṃ saṃskaroti
1.3.2.6	ayam u vai yaḥ pavate sa yajñaḥ
1.3.2.7	tasya manaś ca vāk ca vartanī
1.3.2.8	manasā caiva hi vācā ca yajño vartate
1.3.2.9	ada eva mana iyam eva vāk
1.3.2.10	sa yad vadan nāsti vidyād ardhaṃ me 'sya yajñasyāntaragād iti
1.3.2.11	tad yathaikapāt puruṣo yann ekacakro vā ratho vartamāno bhreṣaṃ nyety evam evāsya yajño bhreṣaṃ nyeti
1.3.2.12	yajñasya bhreṣam anu yajamāno bhreṣaṃ nyeti
1.3.2.13	yajamānasya bhreṣam anv ṛtvijo bhreṣaṃ niyanti
1.3.2.14	ṛtvijāṃ bhreṣam anu dakṣiṇā bhreṣaṃ niyanti
1.3.2.15	dakṣiṇānāṃ bhreṣam anu yajamānaḥ putrapaśubhir bhreṣaṃ nyeti
1.3.2.16	putrapaśūnāṃ bhreṣam anu yajamānaḥ svargeṇa lokena bhreṣaṃ nyeti
1.3.2.17	svargasya lokasya bhreṣam anu tasyārdhasya yogakṣemo bhreṣaṃ nyeti yasminn ardhe yajanta iti brāhmaṇam
1.3.3.1	tad u ha smāha śvetaketur āruṇeyo brahmāṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhāṣamāṇam ardhaṃ me 'sya yajñasyāntaragād iti
1.3.3.2	tasmād brahmā stute bahiḥpavamāne vācoyamyam upāṃśv antaryāmābhyām
1.3.3.3	atha ye pavamānā odṛcas teṣu
1.3.3.4	atha yāni stotrāṇi saśastrāṇy ā vaṣaṭkārāt teṣu
1.3.3.5	sa yad ṛkto bhreṣaṃ nyṛcched oṃ bhūr janad iti gārhapatye juhuyāt
1.3.3.6	yadi yajuṣṭa oṃ bhuvo janad iti dakṣiṇāgnau juhuyāt
1.3.3.7	yadi sāmata oṃ svar janad ity āhavanīye juhuyāt
1.3.3.8	yady anājñātād brahmato voṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svar janad om ity āhavanīya eva juhuyāt
1.3.3.9	tad vākovākyasyarcāṃ yajuṣāṃ sāmnām atharvāṅgirasām
1.3.3.10	athāpi vedānāṃ rasana yajñasya viriṣṭaṃ saṃdhīyate
1.3.3.11	tad yathā lavaṇenety uktam
1.3.3.12	tad yathobhayapāt puruṣo yann ubhayacakro vā ratho vartamāno 'bhreṣaṃ nyeti evam evāsya yajño 'bhreṣaṃ nyeti
1.3.3.13	yajñasyābhreṣam anu yajamāno 'bhreṣaṃ nyeti
1.3.3.14	yajamānasyābhreṣam anv ṛtvijo 'bhreṣaṃ niyanti
1.3.3.15	ṛtvijām abhreṣam anu dakṣiṇā abhreṣaṃ niyanti
1.3.3.16	dakṣiṇānām abhreṣam anu yajamānaḥ putrapaśubhir abhreṣaṃ nyeti
1.3.3.17	putrapaśūnām abhreṣam anu yajamānaḥ svargeṇa lokenābhreṣaṃ nyeti
1.3.3.18	svargasya lokasyābhreṣam anu tasyārdhasya yogakṣemo 'bhreṣaṃ nyeti yasminn ardhe yajanta iti brāhmaṇam
1.3.4.1	tad yad audumbaryāṃ ma āsiṣṭa hiṅṅakārṣīn me prāstāvīn ma udagāsīn me subrahmaṇyām āhvāsīd ity udgātre dakṣiṇā nīyante
1.3.4.2	grahān me 'grahīt prācārīn me 'śuśruvan me samanasas kārṣīd ayākṣīn me 'vaṣaṭkārṣīn ma ity adhvaryave
1.3.4.3	hotṛṣadana āsiṣṭāyākṣīn me 'śāṃsīn me 'vaṣaṭkārṣīn ma iti hotre
1.3.4.4	devayajanaṃ me cīkﾱpad brahmāsādaṃ me 'sīsṛpad brahmajapān me 'japīt purastāddhomasaṃsthitahomān me 'hauṣīd ayākṣīn me 'śāṃsīn me 'vaṣaṭkārṣīn ma iti brahmaṇe
1.3.4.5	bhūyiṣṭhena mā brahmaṇākārṣīd iti
1.3.4.6	etad vai bhūyiṣṭhaṃ brahma yad bhṛgvaṅgirasaḥ
1.3.4.7	ye 'ṅgirasaḥ sa raso ye 'tharvāṇo ye 'tharvāṇas tadbheṣajam
1.3.4.8	yad bheṣajaṃ tad amṛtaṃ yad amṛtaṃ tad brahma
1.3.4.9	sa vā eṣa pūrveṣām ṛtvijām ardhabhāgasyārdham itareṣām ardhaṃ brahmaṇa iti brāhmaṇam
1.3.5.1	devāś ca ha vā asurāś ca saṃgrāmaṃ samayatanta
1.3.5.2	tatraitās tisro hotrā jihmaṃ pratipedire
1.3.5.3	tāsām indra ukthāni sāmāni lulopa
1.3.5.4	tāni hotre prāyacchat
1.3.5.5	ājyaṃ ha vai hotur babhūva
1.3.5.6	praugaṃ potur vaiśvadevaṃ ha vai hotur babhūva
1.3.5.7	niṣkevalyaṃ neṣṭuḥ
1.3.5.8	marutvatīyaṃ ha vai hotur babhūva
1.3.5.9	āgnimārutam āgnīdhrasya
1.3.5.10	tasmād etad abhyastataram iva śasyate yad āgnimārutam
1.3.5.11	tasmād ete saṃśaṃsukā iva bhavanti yaddhotā potā neṣṭā
1.3.5.12	āgnīdhro mumuhe vasīta
1.3.5.13	tad brahmeyasāmivāsa
1.3.5.14	tāsām ardhaṃ pratilulopa prathamārhaṇaṃ ca prathamapadaṃ caitad dakṣiṇāṃ caitat pariśiṣeded iti brāhmaṇam
1.3.6.1	uddālako ha vā āruṇir udīcyān vṛto dhāvayāṃcakāra
1.3.6.2	tasya ha niṣka upāhito babhūvopavādād bibhyato yo mā brāhmaṇo 'nūcāna upavadiṣyati tasmā etaṃ pradāsyāmīti
1.3.6.3	taddhodīcyān brāhmaṇān bhayaṃ vivedoddālako ha vā ayam āyāti kaurupañcālo brahmā brahmaputraḥ
1.3.6.4	sa ūrdhvaṃ vṛto na paryādadhīta
1.3.6.5	kenemaṃ vīreṇa pratisaṃyatāmahā iti
1.3.6.6	taṃ yata eva prapannaṃ dadhre tata evam anupratipedire te ha svaidāyanaṃ śaunakam ūcuḥ svaidāyana tvaṃ vai no brahmiṣṭho 'sīti
1.3.6.7	tvayemaṃ vīreṇa pratisaṃyatāmahā iti
1.3.6.8	taṃ yata eva prapannaṃ dadhre tata evam anupratipedire
1.3.6.9	taṃ ha svaidāyanā ity āmantrayāmāsa
1.3.6.10	sa bho gautamasya putreti hāsmā asūyā pratiśrutaṃ pratiśuśrāva
1.3.6.11	sa vai gautamasya putra ūrdhvaṃ vṛto dhāvet
1.3.7.1	yas tad darśapūrṇamāsayo rūpaṃ vidyāt kasmād imāḥ prajāḥ śirastaḥ prathamaṃ lomaśā jāyante kasmād āsām aparam iva śmaśrūṇy upakakṣāṇy anyāni lomāni jāyante
1.3.7.2	yas tad darśapūrṇamāsayo rūpaṃ vidyāt kasmād imāḥ prajāḥ śirastaḥ prathamaṃ palitā bhavanti kasmād antataḥ sarvā eva palitā bhavanti
1.3.7.3	yas tad darśapūrṇamāsayo rūpaṃ vidyāt kasmād imāḥ prajā adantikā jāyante kasmād āsām aparam iva jāyante
1.3.7.4	yas tad darśapūrṇamāsayo rūpaṃ vidyāt kasmād āsāṃ saptavarṣāṣṭavarṣāṇāṃ prabhidyante kasmād āsāṃ punar eva jāyante kasmād antataḥ sarva eva prabhidyante
1.3.7.5	yas tad darśapūrṇamāsayo rūpaṃ vidyāt kasmād adhare dantāḥ pūrve jāyante para uttare
1.3.7.6	yas tad darśapūrṇamāsayo rūpaṃ vidyāt kasmād adhare dantāḥ aṇīyāṃso hrasīyāṃsaḥ prathīyāṃso varṣīyāṃsa uttare
1.3.7.7	yas tad darśapūrṇamāsayo rūpaṃ vidyāt kasmād imau daṃṣṭrau dīrghatarau kasmāt same iva jambhe
1.3.7.8	yas tad darśapūrṇamāsayo rūpaṃ vidyāt kasmād ime śrotre antarataḥ same iva dīrṇe
1.3.7.9	yas tad darśapūrṇamāsayo rūpaṃ vidyāt kasmāt pumāṃsaḥ śmaśruvanto 'śmaśruvaḥ striyaḥ
1.3.7.10	yas tad darśapūrṇamāsayo rūpaṃ vidyāt kasmād āsāṃ saṃtatam iva śarīraṃ bhavati kasmād āsām asthīni dṛḍhatarāṇīva bhavanti
1.3.7.11	yas tad darśapūrṇamāsayo rūpaṃ vidyāt kasmād āsāṃ prathame vayasi retaḥ siktaṃ na sambhavati kasmād āsāṃ madhyame vayasi retaḥ siktaṃ sambhavati kasmād āsām uttame vayasi retaḥ siktaṃ na sambhavati
1.3.7.12	yas tad darśapūrṇamāsayo rūpaṃ vidyāt kasmād idaṃ śiśnam uccaśa eti nīcī padyate
1.3.7.13	kasmāt sakṛd apānam
1.3.8.1	atha yaḥ purastād aṣṭāv ājyabhāgān vidyān madhyataḥ pañca havirbhāgāḥ ṣaṭ prājāpatyā upariṣṭād aṣṭāv ājyabhāgān vidyāt
1.3.8.2	atha yo gāyatrīṃ hariṇīṃ jyotiṣpakṣāṃ sarvair yajñair yajamānaṃ svargaṃ lokam abhivahantīṃ vidyāt
1.3.8.3	atha yaḥ apaṅktiṃ pañcapadāṃ saptadaśākṣarāṃ sarvair yajñair yajamānaṃ svargaṃ lokam abhivahantīṃ vidyāt
1.3.8.4	tasmai ha niṣkaṃ prayacchann uvācānūcāno ha vai svaidāyanāsi suvarṇaṃ vai suvarṇavide dadāmīti
1.3.8.5	tad upayamya niścakrāma
1.3.8.6	tatrāpavavrāja yatretaro babhūva
1.3.8.7	taṃ ha papraccha kim eṣa gautamasya putra iti
1.3.8.8	eṣa brahmā brahmaputra iti hovāca yad enaṃ kaścid upavadetota mīmāṃseta ha vā mūrdhā vā asya vipatet prāṇā vainaṃ jahyur iti
1.3.8.9	te mitha eva cikrandeyurviprāpavavraja yatretaro babhūva
1.3.8.10	te prātaḥ samitpāṇaya upodeyur upāyāmo bhavantam iti
1.3.8.11	kimartham iti
1.3.8.12	yān eva no bhavāṃs tān hyaḥ praśnān apṛcchat tān eva no bhavān vyācakṣīteti
1.3.8.13	tatheti
1.3.8.14	tebhya etān praśnān vyācacaṣṭe
1.3.9.1	yat purastād vedeḥ prathamaṃ barhi stṛṇāti tasmād imāḥ prajāḥ śirastaḥ prathamaṃ lomaśā jāyante
1.3.9.2	yad aparam iva prastaram anuprastṛṇāti tasmād āsām aparam iva śmaśrūṇy upakakṣāṇy anyāni lomāni jāyante
1.3.9.3	yat prāg barhiṣaḥ prastaram anupraharati tasmād imāḥ prajāḥ śirastaḥ prathamaṃ palitā bhavanti
1.3.9.4	yad antataḥ sarvam evānupraharati tasmād antataḥ sarva eva palitā bhavanti
1.3.9.5	yat prayājā apuronuvākyāvanto bhavanti tasmād imāḥ prajā adantikā jāyante
1.3.9.6	yaddhavīṃṣi puronuvākyāvanti bhavanti tasmād āsām aparam iva jāyante
1.3.9.7	yad anuyājā apuronuvākyāvanto bhavanti tasmād āsāṃ saptavarṣāṣṭavarṣāṇāṃ prabhidyante
1.3.9.8	yat patnīsaṃyājāḥ puronuvākyāvanto bhavanti tasmād āsāṃ punar eva jāyante
1.3.9.9	yat samiṣṭayajur apuronuvākyāvad bhavati tasmād antataḥ sarva eva prabhidyante
1.3.9.10	yad gāyatryānūcya triṣṭubhā yajati tasmād adhare dantāḥ pūrve jāyante para uttare
1.3.9.11	yad ṛcānūcya yajuṣā yajati tasmād adhare dantā aṇīyāṃso hrasīyāṃsaḥ prathīyāṃso varṣīyāṃsa uttare
1.3.9.12	yad āghārau dīrghatarau prāñcāv āghārayati tasmād imau daṃṣṭrau dīrghatarau
1.3.9.13	yat saṃyājye sacchandasī tasmāt same iva jambhe
1.3.9.14	yac caturthe prayāje samānayati tasmād ime śrotre antarataḥ same iva dīrṇe
1.3.9.15	yaj japaṃ japitvābhihiṅkṛṇoti tasmāt pumāṃsaḥ śmaśruvanto 'śmaśruva striyaḥ
1.3.9.16	yat sāmidhenīḥ saṃtanvann anvāha tasmād āsāṃ saṃtatam iva śarīraṃ bhavati
1.3.9.17	yat sāmidhenyaḥ kāṣṭhahaviṣo bhavanti tasmād āsām asthīni dṛḍhatarāṇīva bhavanti
1.3.9.18	yat prayājā ājyahaviṣo bhavanti tasmād āsāṃ prathame vayasi retaḥ siktaṃ na sambhavati
1.3.9.19	yan madhye haviṣāṃ dadhnā ca puroḍāśena ca pracaranti tasmād āsāṃ madhyame vayasi retaḥ siktaṃ sambhavati
1.3.9.20	yad anuyājā ājyahaviṣo bhavanti tasmād āsām uttame vayasi retaḥ siktaṃ na sambhavati
1.3.9.21	yad uttame 'nuyāje sakṛd apāniti tasmād idaṃ śiśnam uccaśa eti nīcī padyate
1.3.9.22	yan nāpānet sakṛcchūnaṃ syāt
1.3.9.23	yan muhur apānet sakṛtpannaṃ syāt
1.3.9.24	tasmāt sakṛd apāniti net sakṛcchūnaṃ syāt sakṛtpannaṃ veti
1.3.10.1	atha ye purastād aṣṭāv ājyabhāgāḥ pañca prayājā dvāv āghārau dvāv ājyabhāgāv āgneya ājyabhāgānāṃ prathamaḥ saumyo dvitīyo havirbhāgānām
1.3.10.2	havir hy eva saumyam
1.3.10.3	āgneyaḥ puroḍāśaḥ
1.3.10.4	agnīṣomīyaḥ puroḍāśo 'gniḥ sviṣṭakṛd ity ete madhyataḥ pañca havirbhāgāḥ
1.3.10.5	atha ye ṣaṭ prājāpatyā iḍā ca prāśitraṃ ca yac cāgnīdhrāyāvadyati brahmabhāgo yajamānabhāgo 'nvāhārya eva ṣaṣṭhaḥ
1.3.10.6	atha ya upariṣṭād aṣṭāv ājyabhāgās trayo 'nuyājāś catvāraḥ patnīsaṃyājāḥ samiṣṭayajur aṣṭamam
1.3.10.7	atha yā gāyatrī hariṇī jyotiṣpakṣā sarvair yajñair yajamānaṃ svargaṃ lokam abhivahati vedir eva sā
1.3.10.8	tasya ye purastād aṣṭāv ājyabhāgāḥ sa dakṣiṇaḥ pakṣaḥ
1.3.10.9	atha ya upariṣṭād aṣṭāv ājyabhāgāḥ sa uttaraḥ pakṣaḥ
1.3.10.10	havīṃṣy ātmā
1.3.10.11	gārhapatyo jaghanam
1.3.10.12	āhavanīyaḥ śiraḥ
1.3.10.13	sauvarṇarājatau pakṣau
1.3.10.14	tad yad ādityaṃ purastāt paryantaṃ na paśyanti tasmād ajyotiṣka utkaro bhavati
1.3.10.15	atha yā paṅktiḥ pañcapadā saptadaśākṣarā sarvair yajñair yajamānaṃ svargaṃ lokam abhivahati yājyaiva sā
1.3.10.16	tasyā oṃ śrāvayeti caturakṣaram
1.3.10.17	astu śrauṣad iti caturakṣaram
1.3.10.18	yajeti dvyakṣaram
1.3.10.19	ye yajāmaha iti pañcākṣaram
1.3.10.20	dvyakṣaro vai vaṣaṭkāraḥ saiṣā paṅktiḥ
1.3.10.21	pañcapadā saptadaśākṣarā sarvair yajñair yajamānaṃ svargaṃ lokam abhivahati
1.3.10.22	tad yatrāsyaiśvaryaṃ syād yatra vainam abhivaheyur evaṃvidam eva tatra brahmāṇaṃ vṛṇīyān nānevaṃvidam iti brāhmaṇam
1.3.11.1	atha ha prācīnayogya ājagāmāgnihotraṃ bhavantaṃ pṛcchāmi gautameti
1.3.11.2	pṛccha prācīnayogyeti
1.3.11.3	kiṃdevatyaṃ te gavīḍāyām
1.3.11.4	kiṃdevatyam upahūtāyām
1.3.11.5	kiṃdevatyam upasṛṣṭāyām
1.3.11.6	kiṃdevatyaṃ vatsam unnīyamānam
1.3.11.7	kiṃdevatyaṃ vatsam unnītam
1.3.11.8	kiṃdevatyaṃ duhyamānam
1.3.11.9	kiṃdevatyaṃ dugdham
1.3.11.10	kiṃdevatyaṃ prakramyamāṇam
1.3.11.11	kiṃdevatyaṃ hriyamāṇam
1.3.11.12	kiṃdevatyam adhiśrīyamāṇam
1.3.11.13	kiṃdevatyam adhiśritam
1.3.11.14	kiṃdevatyam abhyavajvālyamānam
1.3.11.15	kiṃdevatyam abhyavajvālitam
1.3.11.16	kiṃdevatyaṃ samudvāntam
1.3.11.17	kiṃdevatyaṃ viṣyaṇṇam
1.3.11.18	kiṃdevatyam adbhiḥ pratyānītam
1.3.11.19	kiṃdevatyam udvāsyamānam
1.3.11.20	kiṃdevatyam udvāsitam
1.3.11.21	kiṃdevatyam unnīyamānam
1.3.11.22	kiṃdevatyam unnītam
1.3.11.23	kiṃdevatyaṃ prakramyamāṇam
1.3.11.24	kiṃdevatyaṃ hriyamāṇam
1.3.11.25	kiṃdevatyam upasādyamānam
1.3.11.26	kiṃdevatyam upasāditam
1.3.11.27	kiṃdevatyā samit
1.3.11.28	kiṃdevatyāṃ prathamām āhutim ahauṣīḥ
1.3.11.29	kiṃdevatyaṃ gārhapatyam avekṣiṣṭhāḥ
1.3.11.30	kiṃdevatyottarāhutiḥ
1.3.11.31	kiṃdevatyaṃ hutvā srucaṃ trir udañcam udanaiṣīḥ
1.3.11.32	kiṃdevatyaṃ barhiṣi srucaṃ nidhāyonmṛjyottarataḥ pāṇī niramārkṣīḥ
1.3.11.33	kiṃdevatyaṃ dvitīyam unmṛjya pitryupavītaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇataḥ pitṛbhyaḥ svadhām akārṣīḥ
1.3.11.34	kiṃdevatyaṃ prathamaṃ prāśīḥ
1.3.11.35	kiṃdevatyaṃ dvitīyam
1.3.11.36	kiṃdevatyam antataḥ sarvam eva prāśīḥ
1.3.11.37	kiṃdevatyam aprakṣālitayodakaṃ srucā nyanaiṣīḥ
1.3.11.38	kiṃdevatyaṃ prakṣālitayā
1.3.11.39	kiṃdevatyam apareṇāhavanīyam udakaṃ srucā nyanaiṣīḥ
1.3.11.40	kiṃdevatyaṃ sruvaṃ srucaṃ ca pratyatāpsīḥ
1.3.11.41	kiṃdevatyaṃ rātrau srugdaṇḍam avāmārkṣīḥ
1.3.11.42	kiṃdevatyaṃ prātar udamārkṣīr iti
1.3.11.43	etac ced vettha gautama hutaṃ te yady u na vetthāhutaṃ ta iti brāhmaṇam
1.3.12.1	sa hovāca raudraṃ me gavīḍāyām
1.3.12.2	mānavyam upahūtāyām
1.3.12.3	vāyavyam upasṛṣṭāyām
1.3.12.4	vairājaṃ vatsam unnīyamānam
1.3.12.5	jāgatam unnītam
1.3.12.6	āśvinaṃ duhyamānam
1.3.12.7	saumyaṃ dugdham
1.3.12.8	bārhaspatyaṃ prakramyamāṇam
1.3.12.9	dyāvāpṛthivyaṃ hriyamāṇam
1.3.12.10	āgneyam adhiśrīyamāṇam
1.3.12.11	vaiśvānarīyam adhiśritam
1.3.12.12	vaiṣṇavam abhyavajvālyamānam
1.3.12.13	mārutam abhyavajvālitam
1.3.12.14	pauṣṇaṃ samudvāntam
1.3.12.15	vāruṇaṃ viṣyaṇṇam
1.3.12.16	sārasvatam adbhiḥ pratyānītam
1.3.12.17	tvāṣṭram udvāsyamānam
1.3.12.18	dhātram udvāsitam
1.3.12.19	vaiśvadevam unnīyamānam
1.3.12.20	sāvitram unnītam
1.3.12.21	bārhaspatyaṃ prakramyamāṇam
1.3.12.22	dyāvāpṛthivyaṃ hriyamāṇam
1.3.12.23	aindram upasādyamānam
1.3.12.24	balāyopasannam
1.3.12.25	āgneyī samit
1.3.12.26	yāṃ prathamām āhutim ahauṣaṃ mām eva tat svarge loke 'dhām
1.3.12.27	yad gārhapatyam avekṣiṣam asya lokasya saṃtatyai
1.3.12.28	prājāpatyottarāhutiḥ
1.3.12.29	tasmāt pūrṇatarā manasaiva sā
1.3.12.30	yaddhutvā srucaṃ trir udañcam udanaiṣaṃ rudrāṃs tenāpraiṣam
1.3.12.31	yad barhiṣi srucaṃ nidhāyonmṛjyottarataḥ pāṇī niramārkṣam oṣadhivanaspatīṃs tenāpraiṣam
1.3.12.32	yad dvitīyam unmṛjya pitryupavītaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇataḥ pitṛbhyaḥ svadhām akārṣaṃ pitṝṃs tenāpraiṣam
1.3.12.33	yat prathamaṃ prāśiṣaṃ prāṇāṃs tenāpraiṣam
1.3.12.34	yad dvitīyaṃ garbhāṃs tena
1.3.12.35	tasmād anaśnanto garbhā jīvanti
1.3.12.36	yad antataḥ sarvam eva prāśiṣaṃ viśvān devāṃs tenāpraiṣam
1.3.12.37	yad aprakṣālitayodakaṃ srucā nyanaiṣaṃ sarpetarajanāṃs tenāpraiṣam
1.3.12.38	yat prakṣālitayā sarpapuṇyajanāṃs tena
1.3.12.39	yad apareṇāhavanīyam udakaṃ srucā nyanaiṣaṃ gandharvāpsarasas tenāpraiṣam
1.3.12.40	yat sruvaṃ srucaṃ ca pratyatāpsaṃ saptarṣīṃs tenāpraiṣam
1.3.12.41	yad rātrau srugdaṇḍam avāmārkṣaṃ ye rātrau saṃviśanti dakṣiṇāṃs tān udanaiṣam
1.3.12.42	yat prātar udamārkṣaṃ ye prātaḥ pravrajanti dakṣiṇāṃs tānudanaiṣam iti brāhmaṇam
1.3.13.1	evam evaitad bho yathā bhavān āha
1.3.13.2	pṛcchāmi tveva bhavantam iti
1.3.13.3	pṛccha prācīnayogyeti
1.3.13.4	yasya sāyam agnaya upasamāhitāḥ syuḥ sarve jvalayeyuḥ prakṣālitāni yajñapātrāṇy upasannāni syur atha ced dakṣiṇāgnir udvāyāt kiṃ vā tato bhayam āgacched iti
1.3.13.5	kṣipram asya patnī praiti yo 'vidvāñ juhoti
1.3.13.6	vidyayā tvevāham abhijuhomīti
1.3.13.7	kā te vidyā kā prāyaścittir iti
1.3.13.8	gārhapatyād adhi dakṣiṇāgniṃ praṇīya prāco 'ṅgārān uddhṛtya prāṇāpānābhyāṃ svāheti juhuyāt
1.3.13.9	atha prātar yathāsthānam agnīn upasamādhāya yathāpuraṃ juhuyāt
1.3.13.10	sā me vidyā sā prāyaścittir iti
1.3.13.11	atha ced āhavanīya udvāyāt kiṃ vā tato bhayam āgacched iti
1.3.13.12	kṣipram asya putraḥ praiti yo 'vidvāñ juhoti
1.3.13.13	vidyayā tvevāham abhijuhomīti
1.3.13.14	kā te vidyā kā prāyaścittir iti
1.3.13.15	gārhapatyād adhy āhavanīyaṃ praṇīya pratīco 'ṅgārān uddhṛtya samānavyānābhyāṃ svāheti juhuyāt
1.3.13.16	atha prātar yathāsthānam agnīn upasamādhāya yathāpuraṃ juhuyāt
1.3.13.17	sā me vidyā sā prāyaścittir iti
1.3.13.18	atha ced gārhapatya udvāyāt kiṃ vā tato bhayam āgacched iti
1.3.13.19	kṣipraṃ gṛhapatiḥ praiti yo 'vidvāñ juhoti
1.3.13.20	vidyayā tvevāham abhijuhomīti
1.3.13.21	kā te vidyā kā prāyaścittir iti
1.3.13.22	sabhasmakam āhavanīyaṃ dakṣiṇena dakṣiṇāgniṃ parihṛtya gārhapatyasyāyatane pratiṣṭhāpya tata āhavanīyaṃ praṇīya udīco 'ṅgārān uddhṛtyodānarūpābhyāṃ svāheti juhuyāt
1.3.13.23	atha prātar yathāsthānam agnīn upasamādhāya yathāpuraṃ juhuyāt
1.3.13.24	sā me vidyā sā prāyaścittir iti
1.3.13.25	atha cet sarve 'gnaya udvāyeyuḥ kiṃ vā tato bhayam āgacched iti
1.3.13.26	kṣipraṃ gṛhapatiḥ sarvajyāniṃ jīyate yo 'vidvāñ juhoti
1.3.13.27	vidyayā tvevāham abhijuhomīti
1.3.13.28	kā te vidyā kā prāyaścittir iti
1.3.13.29	ānaḍuhena śakṛtpiṇḍenāgnyāyatanāni parilipya homyam upasādyāgniṃ nirmathya prāṇāpānābhyāṃ svāhā samānavyānābhyāṃ svāhodānarūpābhyāṃ svāheti juhuyāt
1.3.13.30	atha prātar yathāsthānam agnīn upasamādhāya yathāpuraṃ juhuyāt
1.3.13.31	sā me vidyā sā prāyaścittir iti
1.3.13.32	atha cen nāgniṃ janayituṃ śaknuyur na kutaścana vāto vāyāt kiṃ vā tato bhayam āgacched iti
1.3.13.33	mogham asyeṣṭaṃ ca hutaṃ ca bhavati yo 'vidvāñ juhoti
1.3.13.34	vidyayā tvevāham abhijuhomīti
1.3.13.35	kā te vidyā kā prāyaścittir iti
1.3.13.36	ānaḍuhenaiva śakṛtpiṇḍenāgnyāyatanāni parilipya homyam upasādya vāta ā vātu bheṣajam iti sūktenātmany eva juhuyāt
1.3.13.37	atha prātar agniṃ nirmathya yathāsthānam agnīn upasamādhāya yathāpuraṃ juhuyāt
1.3.13.38	sā me vidyā sā prāyaścittir iti brāhmaṇam
1.3.14.1	evam evaitad bho bhagavan yathā bhavān āha
1.3.14.2	upayāmi tveva bhavantam iti
1.3.14.3	evaṃ cen nāvakṣyo mūrdhā te vyapatiṣyad iti
1.3.14.4	hanta tu te tad vakṣyāmi yathā te na vipatiṣyatīti
1.3.14.5	yo ha vā evaṃ vidvān aśnāti ca pibati ca vāk tena tṛpyati
1.3.14.6	vāci tṛptāyām agnis tṛpyati
1.3.14.7	agnau tṛpte pṛthivī tṛpyati
1.3.14.8	pṛthivyāṃ tṛptāyāṃ yāni pṛthivyāṃ bhūtāny anvāyattāni tāni tṛpyanti
1.3.14.9	yo ha vā evaṃ vidvān aśnāti ca pibati ca prāṇas tena tṛpyati
1.3.14.10	prāṇe tṛpte vāyus tṛpyati
1.3.14.11	vāyau tṛpte 'ntarikṣaṃ tṛpyati
1.3.14.12	antarikṣe tṛpte yāny antarikṣe bhūtāny anvāyattāni tāni tṛpyanti
1.3.14.13	yo ha vā evaṃ vidvān aśnāti ca pibati ca cakṣus tena tṛpyati
1.3.14.14	cakṣuṣi tṛpta ādityas tṛpyati
1.3.14.15	āditye tṛpte dyaus tṛpyati
1.3.14.16	divi tṛptāyāṃ yāni divi bhūtāny anvāyattāni tāni tṛpyanti
1.3.14.17	yo ha vā evaṃ vidvān aśnāti ca pibati ca manas tena tṛpyati
1.3.14.18	manasi tṛpte candramās tṛpyati
1.3.14.19	candramasi tṛpta āpas tṛpyanti
1.3.14.20	apsu tṛptāsu yāny apsu bhūtāny anvāyattāni tāni tṛpyanti
1.3.14.21	yo ha vā evaṃ vidvān aśnāti ca pibati ca śrotraṃ tena tṛpyati
1.3.14.22	śrotre tṛpte diśaś cāntardeśāś ca tṛpyanti
1.3.14.23	dikṣu cāntardeśeṣu ca tṛpteṣu yāni dikṣu cāntardeśeṣu ca bhūtāny anvāyattāni tāni tṛpyanti
1.3.14.24	yo ha vā evaṃ vidvān aśnāti ca pibati ca tasyāyam eva dakṣiṇaḥ pāṇir juhūḥ
1.3.14.25	savya upabhṛt
1.3.14.26	kaṇṭho dhruvā
1.3.14.27	annaṃ haviḥ
1.3.14.28	prāṇā jyotīṃṣi
1.3.14.29	sadeṣṭaṃ sadā hutaṃ sadāśitaṃ pāyitam agnihotraṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda yaś caivaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhotīti brāhmaṇam
1.3.15.1	priyamedhā ha vai bharadvājā yajñavido manyamānāḥ
1.3.15.2	te ha sma na kaṃcana vedavidam upayanti
1.3.15.3	te sarvam aviduḥ
1.3.15.4	te sahaivāviduḥ
1.3.15.5	te 'gnihotra eva na samavadanta
1.3.15.6	teṣām ekaḥ sakṛd agnihotram ajuhod dvir ekas trir ekaḥ
1.3.15.7	teṣāṃ yaḥ sakṛd agnihotram ajuhot tam itarāv apṛcchatāṃ kasmai tvaṃ juhoṣīti
1.3.15.8	ekadhā vā idaṃ sarvaṃ prajāpatiḥ
1.3.15.9	prajāpataya evāhaṃ sāyaṃ juhomīti prajāpataye prātar iti
1.3.15.10	teṣāṃ yo dvir ajuhot tam itarāv apṛcchatāṃ kābhyāṃ tvaṃ juhoṣīti
1.3.15.11	agnaye prajāpataya iti sāyaṃ sūryāya prajāpataya iti prātaḥ
1.3.15.12	teṣāṃ yas trir ajuhot tam itarāvapṛcchatāṃ kebhyas tvaṃ juhoṣīty agnaye prajāpataye 'numataya iti sāyaṃ sūryāya prajāpataye 'gnaye sviṣṭakṛta iti prātaḥ
1.3.15.13	teṣāṃ yo dvir ajuhot sa ārdhnot

1.4.20.1	tad āhuḥ katham ubhayatojyotiṣo 'bhiplavā anyataratojyotiḥ pṛṣṭhya iti
1.4.20.2	ubhayatojyotiṣo vā ime lokā agnineta ādityenāmuta iti
1.4.20.3	eṣa ha vā eteṣāṃ jyotir ya enaṃ pramṛdīva tapati
1.4.20.4	devacakre ha vā ete pṛṣṭhyapratiṣṭhite pāpmānaṃ tṛṃhatī pariplavete
1.4.20.5	tad ya evaṃ viduṣāṃ dīkṣitānāṃ pāpakaṃ kīrtayed ete evāsya tad devacakre śiraś chindataḥ
1.4.20.6	daśarātram uddhiḥ
1.4.20.7	pṛṣṭhyābhiplavau cakre
1.4.20.8	daśarātram uddhiṃ pṛṣṭhyābhiplavau cakre tantraṃ kurvīteti ha smāha vāsyuḥ
1.4.20.9	tayo stotrāṇi ca śastrāṇi ca saṃcārayet
1.4.20.10	yaḥ saṃcārayet tasmād ime puruṣe prāṇā nānā santa ekodayāccharīram adhivasati yan na saṃcārayet pramāyuko ha yajamānaḥ syāt
1.4.20.11	eṣa ha vai pramāyuko yo 'ndho vā badhiro vā
1.4.20.12	navāgniṣṭomā māsi sampadyante
1.4.20.13	nava vai prāṇāḥ
1.4.20.14	prāṇair yajñas tāyate
1.4.20.15	ekaviṃśatir ukthyāḥ
1.4.20.16	eka ukthyaḥ ṣoḍaśī
1.4.20.17	annaṃ vā ukthyaḥ

1.5.2.1	athāto gādhapratiṣṭhā

1.5.2.6	gādhaṃ pratiṣṭhā caturviṃśam ahar yathopakakṣadaghnaṃ vā kaṇṭhadaghnaṃ vā yato viśramya prasnāyeyus tādṛk tat
1.5.2.7	prasneyo 'bhiplavaḥ

1.5.2.15	jānudaghno dvitīyaḥ

1.5.5.32	etāvanta eva puruṣasya prāṇā iti
1.5.5.33	atra tat samam
1.5.5.34	sapta ca ha vai śatāni viṃśatiś ca saṃvatsarasyāhāni ca rātrayaś ceti

1.5.5.36	atra tat samam
1.5.5.37	caturdaśa ca ha vai śatāni catvāriṃśac ca saṃvatsarasyārdhāhāś cārdharātrayaś ceti
1.5.5.38	etāvanta eva puruṣasya sthūrā māṃsānīti
1.5.5.39	atra tat samam
1.5.5.40	aṣṭāviṃśatiś ca ha vai śatāny aśītiś ca saṃvatsarasya pādāhāś ca pādarātrayaś ceti
1.5.5.41	etāvanta eva puruṣasya snāvā bandhyā iti
1.5.5.42	atra tat samam
1.5.5.43	daśa ca ha vai sahasrāṇy aṣṭau ca śatāni saṃvatsarasya muhūrtā iti
1.5.5.44	etāvanta eva puruṣasya peśaśamarā iti
1.5.5.45	atra tat samam
1.5.5.46	yāvanto muhūrtāḥ pañcadaśa kṛtvas tāvantaḥ prāṇāḥ
