1.5.5.48	yāvanto 'pānāḥ pañcadaśa kṛtvas tāvanto vyānāḥ
1.5.5.49	yāvanto vyānāḥ pañcadaśa kṛtvas tāvantaḥ samānāḥ
1.5.5.50	yāvantaḥ samānāḥ pañcadaśa kṛtvas tāvanta udānāḥ
1.5.5.51	yāvanta udānāḥ pañcadaśa kṛtvas tāvanty etādīni
1.5.5.52	yāvanty etādīni tāvanty etarhīṇi
1.5.5.53	yāvanty etarhīṇi tāvanti svedāyanāni
1.5.5.54	yāvanti svedāyanāni tāvanti kṣiprāyaṇāni
1.5.5.55	yāvanti kṣiprāyaṇāni tāvanto romakūpāḥ
1.5.5.56	yāvanto romakūpāḥ pañcadaśa kṛtvas tāvanto varṣato dhārāḥ
1.5.5.57	tad etat krośaśatikaṃ parimāṇam
1.5.5.58	tad apyetadṛcoktam / śramād anyatra parivartamānaś caran vāsīno yadi vā svapann api / ahorātrābhyāṃ puruṣaḥ kṣaṇena kati kṛtvaḥ prāṇiti cāpāniti ca / śataṃ śatāni parivatsarāṇām aṣṭau ca śatāni saṃvatsarasya muhūrtān yān vadanty ahorātrābhyāṃ puruṣaḥ samena kati kṛtvaḥ prāṇiti cāpāniti ca / iti brāhmaṇam
1.5.6.1	saṃvatsarasya samatā veditavyeti ha smāha vāsyuḥ
1.5.6.2	ekam eva purastād viṣuvato 'tirātram upayanty ekam upariṣṭāt
1.5.6.3	tripañcāśatam eva purastād viṣuvato 'gniṣṭomān upayanti tripañcāśatam upariṣṭāt
1.5.6.4	viṃśatiśatam eva purastād viṣuvata ukthyān upayanti viṃśatiśatam upariṣṭāt
1.5.6.5	ṣaḍ eva purastād viṣuvataḥ ṣoḍaśina upayanti ṣaḍ upariṣṭāt
1.5.6.6	triṃśad eva purastād viṣuvataḥ ṣaḍahān upayanti triṃśad upariṣṭāt
1.5.6.7	saiṣā saṃvatsarasya samatā
1.5.6.8	sa ya evam etāṃ saṃvatsarasya samatāṃ veda saṃvatsareṇa sātmā saloko bhūtvā devān apyetīti brāhmaṇam
1.5.7.1	athāto yajñakramāḥ
1.5.7.2	agnyādheyam
1.5.7.3	agnyādheyātpūrṇāhutiḥ
1.5.7.4	pūrṇāhuteragnihotram
1.5.7.5	agnihotrāddarśapūrṇamāsau
1.5.7.6	darśapūrṇamāsābhyām āgrayaṇam
1.5.7.7	āgrayaṇāccāturmāsyāni
1.5.7.8	cāturmāsyebhyaḥ paśubandhaḥ
1.5.7.9	paśubandhādagniṣṭomaḥ
1.5.7.10	agniṣṭomādrājasūyaḥ
1.5.7.11	rājasūyādvājapeyaḥ
1.5.7.12	vājapeyādaśvamedhaḥ
1.5.7.13	aśvamedhātpuruṣamedhaḥ
1.5.7.14	puruṣamedhātsarvamedhaḥ
1.5.7.15	sarvamedhāddakṣiṇāvantaḥ
1.5.7.16	dakṣiṇāvadbhyo 'dakṣiṇāḥ
1.5.7.17	adakṣiṇāḥ sahasradakṣiṇe pratyatiṣṭhan
1.5.7.18	te vā ete yajñakramāḥ
1.5.7.19	sa ya evam etān yajñakramān veda yajñena sātmā saloko bhūtvā devān apyetīti brāhmaṇam
1.5.8.1	prajāpatir akāmayatānantyam aśnuvīyeti
1.5.8.2	so 'gnīn ādhāya pūrṇāhutyāyajata
1.5.8.3	so 'ntam evāpaśyat
1.5.8.4	so 'gnihotreṇeṣṭvāntam evāpaśyat
1.5.8.5	sa darśapūrṇamāsābhyām iṣṭvāntam evāpaśyat
1.5.8.6	sa āgrayaṇeneṣṭvāntam evāpaśyat
1.5.8.7	sa cāturmāsyair iṣṭvāntam evāpaśyat
1.5.8.8	sa paśubandheneṣṭvāntam evāpaśyat
1.5.8.9	so 'gniṣṭomeneṣṭvāntam evāpaśyat
1.5.8.10	sa rājasūyeneṣṭvā rājeti nāmādhatta
1.5.8.11	so 'ntam evāpaśyat
1.5.8.12	sa vājapeyeneṣṭvā samrāḍ iti nāmādhatta
1.5.8.13	so 'ntam evāpaśyat
1.5.8.14	so 'śvamedheneṣṭvā svarāḍ iti nāmādhatta
1.5.8.15	so 'ntam evāpaśyat
1.5.8.16	sa puruṣamedheneṣṭvā virāḍ iti nāmādhatta
1.5.8.17	so 'ntam evāpaśyat
1.5.8.18	sa sarvamedheneṣṭvā sarvarāḍ iti nāmādhatta
1.5.8.19	so 'ntam evāpaśyat
1.5.8.20	so 'hīnair dakṣiṇāvadbhir iṣṭvāntam evāpaśyat
1.5.8.21	so 'hīnair adakṣiṇāvadbhir iṣṭvāntam evāpaśyat
1.5.8.22	sa sattreṇobhayato 'tirātreṇāntato 'yajata
1.5.8.23	vācaṃ ha vai hotre prāyacchat prāṇam adhvaryave cakṣur udgātre mano brahmaṇe 'ṅgāni hotrakebhya ātmānaṃ sadasyebhyaḥ
1.5.8.24	evam ānantyam ātmānaṃ dattvānantyam āśnuta
1.5.8.25	tad yā dakṣiṇā ānayat tābhir ātmānaṃ niṣkrīṇīya
1.5.8.26	tasmād etena jyotiṣṭomenāgniṣṭomenātmaniṣkrayaṇena sahasradakṣiṇena pṛṣṭhaśamanīyena tvareta
1.5.8.27	yo hyaniṣṭvā pṛṣṭhaśamanīyena praityātmānaṃ so 'niṣkrīya praitīti brāhmaṇam
1.5.9.1	yad vai saṃvatsarāya saṃvatsarasado dīkṣante katham eṣām agnihotram anantaritaṃ bhavati
1.5.9.2	vrateneti brūyāt
1.5.9.3	katham eṣāṃ darśo 'nantarito bhavati
1.5.9.4	dadhnā ca puroḍāśena ceti brūyāt
1.5.9.5	katham eṣāṃ paurṇamāsam anantaritaṃ bhavati
1.5.9.6	ājyena ca puroḍāśena ceti brūyāt
1.5.9.7	katham eṣām āgrayaṇam anantaritaṃ bhavati
1.5.9.8	saumyena caruṇeti brūyāt
1.5.9.9	katham eṣāṃ cāturmāsyāny anantaritāni bhavanti
1.5.9.10	payasyayeti brūyāt
1.5.9.11	katham eṣāṃ paśubandho 'nantarito bhavati
1.5.9.12	paśunā ca puroḍāśena ceti brūyāt
1.5.9.13	katham eṣāṃ saumyo 'dhvaro 'nantarito bhavati
1.5.9.14	grahair iti brūyāt
1.5.9.15	katham eṣāṃ gṛhamedho 'nantarito bhavati
1.5.9.16	dhānākarambhair iti brūyāt
1.5.9.17	katham eṣāṃ pitṛyajño 'nantarito bhavati
1.5.9.18	aupāsanair iti brūyāt
1.5.9.19	katham eṣāṃ mithunam anantaritaṃ bhavati
1.5.9.20	hiṃkāreneti brūyāt
1.5.9.21	saiṣā saṃvatsare yajñakratūnām apītiḥ
1.5.9.22	sa ya evam etāṃ saṃvatsare yajñakratūnām apītiṃ veda yajñena sātmā saloko bhūtvā devān apyetīti brāhmaṇam
1.5.10.1	devā ha vai sahasrasaṃvatsarāya didīkṣire
1.5.10.2	teṣāṃ pañca śatāni saṃvatsarāṇāṃ paryupetāny āsann athedaṃ sarvaṃ śaśrāma ye stomā yāni pṛṣṭhāni yāni śastrāṇi
1.5.10.3	te devā ihasāmivāsurupa taṃ yajñakratuṃ jānīmo yaḥ sahasrasaṃvatsarasya pratimā
1.5.10.4	ko hi tasmai manuṣyo yaḥ sahasrasaṃvatsareṇa yajeteti
1.5.10.5	tad ayātayāma madhye yajñasyāpaśyan
1.5.10.6	tenāyātayāmnā yā vede vyaṣṭir āsīt tāṃ pañcasv apaśyann ṛci yajuṣi sāmni śānte 'tha ghore
1.5.10.7	tā vā etāḥ pañca vyāhṛtayo bhavanty o śrāvayāstu śrauṣaḍ yaja ye yajāmahe vauṣaḍ iti
1.5.10.8	te devā ihasāmivāsurupa taṃ yajñakratuṃ jānīmo yaḥ sahasrasaṃvatsarasya pratimā
1.5.10.9	ko hi tasmai manuṣyo yaḥ sahasrasaṃvatsareṇa yajeteti
1.5.10.10	tata etaṃ tāpaścitaṃ sahasrasaṃvatsarasyāñjasyam apaśyan
1.5.10.11	te hyeva stomā bhavanti tāni pṛṣṭhāni tāni śastrāṇi
1.5.10.12	sa khalu dvādaśa māsān dīkṣābhir eti dvādaśamāsān upasadbhir dvādaśamāsāṃt sutyābhiḥ
1.5.10.13	atha yad dvādaśa māsān dīkṣābhir eti dvādaśamāsān upasadbhis tenaitāvagnyarkāvāpnoti
1.5.10.14	atha yad dvādaśa māsāṃt sutyābhis tenedaṃ mahaduktham avāpnoti
1.5.10.15	te devā ihasāmivāsurupa taṃ yajñakratuṃ jānīmo yaḥ sahasrasaṃvatsarasya pratimā
1.5.10.16	ko hi tasmai manuṣyo yaḥ sahasrasaṃvatsareṇa yajeteti
1.5.10.17	tata etaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ tāpaścitasyāñjasyam apaśyan
1.5.10.18	te hy eva stomā bhavanti tāni pṛṣṭhāni tāni śastrāṇi
1.5.10.19	te devā ihasāmivāsurupa taṃ yajñakratuṃ jānīmo yaḥ sahasrasaṃvatsarasya pratimā
1.5.10.20	ko hi tasmai manuṣyo yaḥ sahasrasaṃvatsareṇa yajeteti
1.5.10.21	tata etaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ saṃvatsarasyāñjasyam apaśyan
1.5.10.22	te hy eva stomā bhavanti tāni pṛṣṭhāni tāni śastrāṇi
1.5.10.23	sa khalu dvādaśāhaṃ dīkṣābhir eti dvādaśāham upasadbhir dvādaśāhaṃ sutyābhiḥ
1.5.10.24	atha yad dvādaśāhaṃ dīkṣābhir eti dvādaśāham upasadbhis tenaitāv agnyarkāv āpnoti
1.5.10.25	atha yad dvādaśāhaṃ sutyābhis tenedaṃ mahaduktham avāpnoti
1.5.10.26	te devā ihasāmivāsurupa taṃ yajñakratuṃ jānīmo yaḥ sahasrasaṃvatsarasya pratimā
1.5.10.27	ko hi tasmai manuṣyo yaḥ sahasrasaṃvatsareṇa yajeteti
1.5.10.28	tata etaṃ pṛṣṭhyaṃ ṣaḍahaṃ dvādaśāhasyāñjasyam apaśyan
1.5.10.29	te hy eva stomā bhavanti tāni pṛṣṭhāni tāni śastrāṇi
1.5.10.30	te devā ihasāmivāsurupa taṃ yajñakratuṃ jānīmo yaḥ sahasrasaṃvatsarasya pratimā
1.5.10.31	ko hi tasmai manuṣyo yaḥ sahasrasaṃvatsareṇa yajeteti
1.5.10.32	tata etaṃ viśvajitaṃ pṛṣṭhyaṣaḍahasyāñjasyam apaśyan
1.5.10.33	te hy eva stomā bhavanti tāni pṛṣṭhāni tāni śastrāṇi
1.5.10.34	te devā ihasāmivāsurupa taṃ yajñakratuṃ jānīmo yaḥ sahasrasaṃvatsarasya pratimā
1.5.10.35	ko hi tasmai manuṣyo yaḥ sahasrasaṃvatsareṇa yajeteti
1.5.10.36	sa vā eṣa viśvajid yaḥ sahasrasaṃvatsarasya pratimā
1.5.10.37	eṣa ha prajānāṃ prajāpatir yad viśvajid iti brāhmaṇam
1.5.11.1	puruṣaṃ ha vai nārāyaṇaṃ prajāpatir uvāca yajasva yajasveti
1.5.11.2	sa hovāca yajasva yajasvety evaṃ hāttha mā
1.5.11.3	trir apikṣata me vasavaḥ prātaḥsavanenāgū rudrā mādhyaṃdinasavanenādityās tṛtīyasavanena
1.5.11.4	yajñavāstuny eva paryaśiṣo yajñavāstum ity evam āśiṣo 'haṃ vā etad veda yajñe vasavaḥ prātaḥsavanenāgū rudrā mādhyaṃdinasavanenādityās tṛtīyasavanena yajñavāstuny eva paryaśiṣo yajñavāstum ity evam āśiṣo vidvāṃso nūnaṃ tvā yājayeyuḥ
1.5.11.5	ete ha vā avidvāṃso yatrānṛgviddhotā bhavaty ayajurvid adhvaryur asāmavid udgātābhṛgvaṅgirovid brahmā
1.5.11.6	yajasvaiva hanta tu te tad vakṣyāmi
1.5.11.7	yathā sūtre maṇir iva sūtram etāny ukthāhāni bhavanti sūtram iva vā maṇāv iti
1.5.11.8	tasmād ya eva sarvavit syāt taṃ brahmāṇaṃ kurvīta
1.5.11.9	eṣa ha vai vidvāṃt sarvavid brahmā yad bhṛgvaṅgirovit
1.5.11.10	ete ha vā asya sarvasya śamayitāraḥ pālayitāraḥ
1.5.11.11	tasmād brahmā stute bahiṣpavamāne vācayati
1.5.12.1	śyeno 'si gāyatrachandāḥ / anu tvārabhe / svasti mā saṃpārayeti
1.5.12.2	sa yad āha śyeno 'sīti somaṃ vā etad āha
1.5.12.3	eṣa ha vā agnir bhūtvāsmiṃlloke saṃśāyayati
1.5.12.4	tad yat saṃśāyayati tasmācchyenaḥ
1.5.12.5	tacchyenasya śyenatvam
1.5.12.6	sa yad āha gāyatrachandā anu tvārabha iti gāyatreṇa chandasā vasubhir devaiḥ prātaḥsavane 'smiṃlloke 'gniṃ santam anvārabhate
1.5.12.7	sa yad āha svasti mā saṃpārayeti gāyatreṇaiva chandasā vasubhir devaiḥ prātaḥsavane 'smiṃlloke 'gninā devena svasti mā saṃpārayeti gāyatreṇaivainaṃ tacchandasā vasubhir devaiḥ prātaḥsavane 'smiṃlloke 'gninā devena svasti sampadyate ya evaṃ veda
1.5.13.1	atha mādhyaṃdine pavamāne vācayati samrāḍ asi triṣṭupchandāḥ / anu tvārabhe / svasti mā saṃpārayeti
1.5.13.2	sa yad āha samrāḍ asīti somaṃ vā etad āha
1.5.13.3	eṣa ha vai vāyurbhūtvāntarikṣaloke saṃrājati
1.5.13.4	tad yat saṃrājati tasmāt samrāṭ
1.5.13.5	tat saṃrājasya samrāṭtvam
1.5.13.6	sa yad āha triṣṭupchandā anu tvārabha iti traiṣṭubhena chandasā rudrair devair mādhyaṃdine savane 'ntarikṣaloke vāyuṃ santam anvārabhate
1.5.13.7	sa yad āha svasti mā saṃpārayeti traiṣṭubhenaiva chandasā rudrair devair mādhyaṃdine savane antarikṣaloke vāyunā devena svasti mā saṃpārayeti
1.5.13.8	traiṣṭubhenaivainaṃ tacchandasā rudrair devair mādhyaṃdine savane antarikṣaloke vāyunā devena svasti sampadyate ya evaṃ veda
1.5.14.1	athārbhave pavamāne vācayati svaro 'si gayo 'si jagacchandāḥ / anu tvārabhe / svasti mā saṃpārayeti
1.5.14.2	sa yad āha svaro 'sīti somaṃ vā etad āha
1.5.14.3	eṣa ha vai sūryo bhūtvāmuṣmiṃlloke svarati
1.5.14.4	tad yat svarati tasmāt svaraḥ
1.5.14.5	tat svarasya svaratvam
1.5.14.6	sa yad āha gayo 'sīti somaṃ vā etad āha
1.5.14.7	eṣa ha vai candramā bhūtvā sarvāṃllokān gacchati
1.5.14.8	tad yad gacchati tasmād gayaḥ
1.5.14.9	tad gayasya gayatvam
1.5.14.10	sa yad āha jagacchandā anu tvārabha iti jāgatena chandasādityair devais tṛtīyasavane 'muṣmiṃlloke sūryaṃ santam anvārabhate
1.5.14.11	sa yad āha svasti mā saṃpārayeti jāgatenaiva chandasādityair devais tṛtīyasavane 'muṣmiṃlloke sūryeṇa devena svasti mā saṃpārayeti jāgatenaivainaṃ tacchandasādityair devais tṛtīyasavane 'muṣmiṃlloke sūryeṇa devena svasti sampadyate ya evaṃ veda
1.5.15.1	atha saṃsthite saṃsthite savane vācayati mayi bhargo mayi maho mayi yaśo mayi sarvam iti
1.5.15.2	pṛthivy eva bhargo 'ntarikṣa eva maho dyaur eva yaśo 'pa eva sarvam
1.5.15.3	agnir eva bhargo vāyur eva maha āditya eva yaśaś candramā eva sarvam
1.5.15.4	vasava eva bhargo rudrā eva maha ādityā eva yaśo viśvedevā eva sarvam
1.5.15.5	gāyatry eva bhargas triṣṭub eva maho jagaty eva yaśo 'nuṣṭub eva sarvam
1.5.15.6	prācy eva bhargaḥ pratīcy eva maha udīcy eva yaśo dakṣiṇaiva sarvam
1.5.15.7	vasanta eva bhargo grīṣma eva maho varṣā eva yaśaḥ śarad eva sarvam
1.5.15.8	trivṛd eva bhargaḥ pañcadaśa eva mahaḥ saptadaśa eva yaśa ekaviṃśa eva sarvam
1.5.15.9	ṛgveda eva bhargo yajurveda eva mahaḥ sāmaveda eva yaśo brahmaveda eva sarvam
1.5.15.10	hotaiva bhargo 'dhvaryur eva maha udgātaiva yaśo brahmaiva sarvam
1.5.15.11	vāg eva bhargaḥ prāṇa eva mahaś cakṣur eva yaśo mana eva sarvam
1.5.16.1	sa yad āha mayi bharga iti pṛthivīm evaitallokānām āhāgniṃ devānāṃ vasūn devān devagaṇānāṃ gāyatraṃ chandasāṃ prācīṃ diśāṃ vasantam ṛtūnāṃ trivṛtaṃ stomānām ṛgvedaṃ vedānāṃ hautraṃ hotrakāṇāṃ vācam indriyāṇām
1.5.17.1	sa yad āha mayi maha ity antarikṣam evaitallokānām āha vāyuṃ devānāṃ rudrān devān devagaṇānāṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ chandasāṃ pratīcīṃ diśāṃ grīṣmam ṛtūnāṃ pañcadaśaṃ stomānāṃ yajurvedaṃ vedānām ādhvaryavaṃ hotrakāṇāṃ prāṇam indriyāṇām
1.5.18.1	sa yad āha mayi yaśa iti divam evaitallokānām āhādityaṃ devānām ādityān devagaṇānāṃ jāgataṃ chandasām udīcīṃ diśāṃ varṣā ṛtūnāṃ saptadaśaṃ stomānāṃ sāmavedaṃ vedānām audgātraṃ hotrakāṇāṃ cakṣur indriyāṇām
1.5.19.1	sa yad āha mayi sarvam ity apa evaitallokānām āha candramasaṃ devānāṃ viśvān devān devagaṇānām ānuṣṭubhaṃ chandasāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ diśāṃ śaradam ṛtūnām ekaviṃśaṃ stomānāṃ brahmavedaṃ vedānāṃ brahmatvaṃ hotrakāṇāṃ mana indriyāṇām
1.5.20.1	sa vā eṣa daśadhā catuḥ sampadyate
1.5.20.2	daśa ca ha vai catur virājo 'kṣarāṇi
1.5.20.3	taṃ garbhā upajīvanti
1.5.20.4	śrīr vai virāṭ
1.5.20.5	yaśo 'nnādyam
1.5.20.6	śriyam eva tad virājaṃ yaśasy annādye pratiṣṭhāpayati
1.5.20.7	pratiṣṭhantīr idaṃ sarvam anupratiṣṭhati
1.5.20.8	pratitiṣṭhati prajayā paśubhir ya evaṃ veda
1.5.21.1	anarvāṇaṃ ha vai devaṃ dadhyaṅṅ āṅgirasa upasīdaṃ ha yajñasya śnuṣṭiṃ samaśnavāmaha iti
1.5.21.2	sa dadhyaṅṅ āṅgiraso 'bravīd yo vai saptadaśaṃ prajāpatiṃ yajñe 'nvitaṃ veda nāsya yajño riṣyate
1.5.21.3	na yajñapatiṃ riṣyanta iti
1.5.21.4	tā vā etāḥ pañca vyāhṛtayo bhavanty o śrāvayāstu śrauṣaḍ yaja ye yajāmahe vauṣaḍ iti
1.5.21.5	sa dadhyaṅṅ āṅgiraso 'bravīn na vayaṃ vidmo yadi brāhmaṇāḥ smo yady abrāhmaṇāḥ smo yadi tasyarṣeḥ smo vānyasyeti
1.5.21.6	anarvāṇaś ca ha vā ṛtāvantaś ca pitaraḥ svadhāyām āvṛṣāyanta vayaṃ vadāmahai vayaṃ vadāmahā iti
1.5.21.7	so 'yāt svāyaṃbhuvo vā ṛtāvanto madayātāṃ na vayaṃ vadāmahā iti
1.5.21.8	tasmāt pravare pravriyamāṇe vācayed devāḥ pitara iti tisraḥ
1.5.21.9	ya eti saṃyajati sa bhavati yaś ca na brūte yaś ca na brūta iti brāhmaṇam
1.5.22.1	sāvitraṃ ha smaitaṃ pūrve purastāt paśum ālabhanta ity etarhi prājāpatyam
1.5.22.2	yo hy eva savitā sa prajāpatir iti vadantaḥ
1.5.22.3	tasmād u samupyāgnīṃs tena yajeran
1.5.22.4	te samānadhiṣṇyā eva syur okhāsaṃbharaṇīyāyāḥ
1.5.22.5	ukhāsaṃbharaṇīyāyāṃ vinyupyāgnīṃs tayā yajeran
1.5.22.6	te nānādhiṣṇyā eva syur ā dīkṣaṇīyāyāḥ
1.5.22.7	dīkṣaṇīyāyāṃ saṃnyupyāgnīṃs tayā yajeran
1.5.22.8	te samānadhiṣṇyā eva syur odavasānīyāyāḥ
1.5.22.9	udavasānīyāyāṃ vinyupyāgnīṃs tayā yajeran
1.5.22.10	te nānādhiṣṇyā eva syuḥ
1.5.22.11	atha yadi yajamānasyopatapet pārśvato 'gnīn ādhāya tāvad āsīta yāvad agadaḥ syāt
1.5.22.12	yadi preyāt svair eva tam agnibhir dahet
1.5.22.13	aśavāgnibhir itare yajamānā āsata iti vadantaḥ
1.5.22.14	tasya tad eva brāhmaṇaṃ yad adaḥ puraḥsavane
1.5.22.15	pitṛmedha āśiṣo vyākhyātāḥ
1.5.23.1	sāyaṃprātarhomau sthālīpāko navaś ca yaḥ / baliś ca pitṛyajñaś cāṣṭakā saptamaḥ paśuḥ / ity ete pākayajñāḥ
1.5.23.2	agnyādheyam agnihotraṃ paurṇamāsyamāvāsye / naveṣṭiś cāturmāsyāni paśubandho 'tra saptamaḥ / ity ete haviryajñāḥ
1.5.23.3	agniṣṭomo 'tyagniṣṭoma ukthyaḥ ṣoḍaśimāṃs tataḥ / vājapeyo 'tirātraś cāptoryāmātra saptamaḥ / ity ete sutyāḥ
1.5.23.4	ke svid devāḥ pravovājāḥ ke svid devā abhidyavaḥ / ke svid devā haviṣmantaḥ kiṃ svij jigāti sumnayuḥ
1.5.23.5	ṛtava eva pravovājā māsā devā abhidyavaḥ / ardhamāsā haviṣmantas taj jigāti sumnayuḥ
1.5.23.6	kati svid rātrayaḥ katy ahāni kati stotrāṇi kati śastrāṇy asya / kati svit savanāḥ saṃvatsarasya stotriyāḥ padākṣarāṇi katy asya
1.5.23.7	dvāv atirātrau ṣaṭ śatam agniṣṭomā dve viṃśatiśate ukthyānāṃ / dvādaśa ṣoḍaśinaḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ ṣaḍahā vaiṣuvataṃ ca
1.5.23.8	ahānyasya viṃśatiśatāni trīṇy ahaś caikaṃ tāvad asya / saṃvatsarasya savanāḥ sahasram asīti trīṇi ca saṃstutasya
1.5.23.9	ṣaṭṣaṣṭiś ca dve ca śate bhavata stutaśastrāṇām ayutaṃ caikam asya / stotriyāś ca navatisahasrā dve niyute navatiś cāti ṣaṭ ca
1.5.23.10	aṣṭau śatāny ayutāni triṃśac caturnavatiś ca padāny asya / saṃvatsarasya kavibhir mitasyaitāvatī madhyamā devamātrā
1.5.23.11	ayutam ekaṃ prayutāni triṃśad dve niyute tathā hy anusṛṣṭāḥ / aṣṭau śatāni nava cākṣarāṇy etāvān ātmā paramaḥ prajāpateḥ
1.5.23.12	ādyaṃ vaṣaṭkāraḥ pradānāntam etam agniṣṭome parvaśaḥ sādhu kﾱptam / saubheṣajaṃ chanda īpsan yad agnau catuḥśataṃ bahudhā hūyate yat
1.5.23.13	prātaḥsavanastuta ekaviṃśo gāyatrastomamita eka eva / mādhyaṃdinaḥ saptadaśena kﾱptas trayastriṃśena savanaṃ tṛtīyam
1.5.24.1	śraddhāyāṃ retas tapasā tapasvī vaiśvānaraḥ siṣice 'patyam īpsan / tato jajñe lokajit somajambhā ṛṣer ṛṣir aṅgirāḥ saṃbabhūva
1.5.24.2	ṛṣer yajñasya caturvidhasya śraddhāṃ yaḥ śreyasīṃ lokam amuṃ jigāya / yasmai vedāḥ prasṛtāḥ somabinduyuktā vahanti sukṛtām u lokam
1.5.24.3	ṛco 'sya bhāgāṃś caturo vahanty ukthaśastraiḥ pramudo modamānāḥ / grahair havirbhiś ca kṛtākṛtaś ca yajūṃṣi bhāgāṃś caturo vahanti
1.5.24.4	audumbaryāṃ sāmaghoṣeṇa tāvat saviṣṭutibhiś ca stomaiḥ chandasā / sāmāni bhāgāṃś caturo vahanti gītyā stomena saha prastāvena ca
1.5.24.5	prāyaścittair bheṣajaiḥ saṃstuvanto 'tharvāṇo 'ṅgirasaś ca śāntāḥ / brahmā brahmatvena pramudo modamānā asaṃsṛṣṭān bhāgāṃś caturo vahanti
1.5.24.6	yo brahmavit so 'bhikaro 'stu vaḥ śivo dhiyā dhīro rakṣatu dharmam etam / mā vaḥ pramattām amṛtāc ca yajñāt karmācca yenānaṅgiraso 'piyāsīt
1.5.24.7	māyuṃ daśaṃ māruśastāḥ prameṣṭā mā me bhūr yuktā vidahātha lokān / divyaṃ bhayaṃ rakṣata dharmam udyataṃ yajñaṃ kālāśa stutigopanāyanam
1.5.24.8	hotā ca maitrāvaruṇaś ca pādam acchāvākaḥ saha grāvastutaikam / ṛgbhi stuvanto 'harahaḥ pṛthivyā agniṃ pādaṃ brahmaṇā dhārayanti
1.5.24.9	adhvaryuḥ pratiprasthātā neṣṭonnetā nihitaṃ pādam ekam / sam antarikṣaṃ yajuṣā stuvanto vāyuṃ pādaṃ brahmaṇā dhārayanti
1.5.24.10	sāmnodgātā chādayann apramatta audumbaryāṃ stobhadeyaḥ sagadgadaḥ / vidvān prastotā vidahātha suṣṭutiṃ subrahmaṇyaḥ pratihartātha yajñe
1.5.24.11	sāmnā divy ekaṃ nihitaṃ stuvantaḥ sūryaṃ pādaṃ brahmaṇā dhārayanti / brahmā haikaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsinaḥ saha potāgnīdhro nihitaṃ pādam ekam
1.5.24.12	atharvabhir aṅgirobhiś ca gupto 'psu candraṃ pādaṃ brahmaṇā dhārayanti / ṣoḍaśikaṃ hotrakā abhiṣṭuvanti vedeṣu yuktāḥ prapṛthak caturdhā
1.5.24.13	manīṣiṇo dīkṣitāḥ śraddadhānā hotāro guptā abhivahanti yajñam / dakṣiṇato brahmaṇasyoṃ janad ity etāṃ vyāhṛtiṃ japan
1.5.24.14	saptadaśaṃ sadasyaṃ taṃ kīrtayanti purā viduḥ / aṣṭādaśī dīkṣitā dīkṣitānāṃ yajñe patnī śraddadhāneha yuktā
1.5.24.15	ekonaviṃśaḥ śamitā babhūva viṃśo yajñe gṛhapatir eva sunvan / ekaviṃśatir evaiṣāṃ saṃsthāyām aṅgiro vaha
1.5.24.16	vedair abhiṣṭuto loko nānāveśāparājitaḥ
1.5.25.1	sapta sutyāḥ sapta ca pākayajñāḥ haviryajñāḥ sapta tathaikaviṃśatiḥ / sarve te yajñā aṅgiraso 'piyanti nūtanā yān ṛṣayo sṛjanti ye ca sṛṣṭāḥ purāṇaiḥ
1.5.25.2	eteṣu vedeṣv api caikam evāpavrajam ṛtvijāṃ saṃbharanti / kṛṭstṛpāt sacate tām aśastiṃ viṣkandham enaṃ visṛtaṃ prajāsu
1.5.25.3	nivartante dakṣiṇā nīyamānāḥ sute some vitate yajñatantre / moghāśiṣo yanty anivartamānā aniṣṭayajñā na taranti lokān
1.5.25.4	dvādaśavarṣaṃ brahmacaryaṃ pṛthag vedeṣu tat smṛtam / evaṃ vyavasthitā vedāḥ sarva eva svakarmasu
1.5.25.5	santi caiṣāṃ samānāḥ mantrāḥ kalpāś ca brāhmaṇāni ca / vyavasthānaṃ tu tat sarvaṃ pṛthagvedeṣu tat smṛtam
1.5.25.6	ṛgvedasya pṛthivī sthānam antarikṣasthāno 'dhvaraḥ / dyau sthānaṃ sāmavedasyāpo bhṛgvaṅgirasāṃ smṛtam
1.5.25.7	agnir devata ṛgvedasya yajurvedo vāyudevataḥ / ādityaḥ sāmavedasya candramā vaidyutaś ca bhṛgvaṅgirasām
1.5.25.8	trivṛtstoma ṛgvedasya yajūṃṣi pañcadaśena saha jajñire / saptadaśena sāmaveda ekaviṃśo brahmasaṃmitaḥ
1.5.25.9	vāg adhyātmam ṛgvedasya yajuṣāṃ prāṇa ucyate / cakṣuṣī sāmavedasya mano bhṛgvaṅgirasāṃ smṛtam
1.5.25.10	ṛgbhiḥ saha gāyatraṃ jāgatam āhur yajūṃṣi traiṣṭubhena saha jajñire / uṣṇikkakubbhyāṃ bhṛgvaṅgiraso jagatyā sāmāni kavayo vadanti
1.5.25.11	ṛgbhiḥ pṛthivīṃ yajuṣāntarikṣaṃ sāmnā divaṃ lokajit somajambhāḥ / atharvabhir aṅgirobhiś ca gupto yajñaś catuṣpād divam udvaheta
1.5.25.12	ṛgbhiḥ suśasto yajuṣā pariṣkṛtaḥ saviṣṭutaḥ sāmajit somajambhāḥ / atharvabhir aṅgirobhiś ca gupto yajñaś catuṣpād divam āruroha
1.5.25.13	ṛco vidvān pṛthivīṃ veda saṃprati yajūṃṣi vidvān bṛhad antarikṣam / divaṃ veda sāmago yo vipaścit sarvān lokān yad bhṛgvaṅgirovit
1.5.25.14	yāṃś ca grāme yāṃś cāraṇye japanti mantrān nānārthān bahudhā janāsaḥ / sarve te yajñā aṅgiraso 'piyanti nūtanā sā hi gatir brahmaṇo yāvarārdhyā
1.5.25.15	triviṣṭapaṃ tridivaṃ nākam uttamaṃ tam etayā trayyā vidyayaiti / ata uttare brahmalokā mahānto 'tharvaṇām aṅgirasāṃ ca sā gatiḥ
1.5.25.16	atharvaṇām aṅgirasāṃ ca sā gatir iti brāhmaṇam
2.1.1.1	atha yad brahmasadanāt tṛṇaṃ nirasyati śodhayaty evainaṃ tat

2.1.1.4	tamevaitat pūrvaṃ sādayati
2.1.1.5	ariṣṭaṃ yajñaṃ tanutād iti

2.1.1.8	tasminn evaitad anujñām icchati praṇītāsu praṇīyamānāsu vācaṃ yacchaty ā haviṣkṛta udvādanāt
2.1.1.9	etad vai yajñasya dvāram

2.1.2.5	tad āviddhaṃ nirakṛntat

2.1.2.36	sa etaṃ mantram apaśyat
2.1.2.37	sūryasya tvā cakṣuṣā pratīkṣa ity abravīt
2.1.2.38	na hi sūryasya cakṣuḥ kiṃcana hinasti
2.1.2.39	so 'bibhet pratigṛhṇantaṃ mā hiṃsiṣyatīti
2.1.2.40	devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ prasūtaḥ praśiṣā pratigṛhṇāmīty abravīt
2.1.2.41	savitṛprasūta evainaṃ tad devatābhiḥ pratyagṛhṇāt
2.1.2.42	tad vyūhya tṛṇāni prāgdaṇḍaṃ sthaṇḍile nidadhāti pṛthivyās tvā nābhau sādayāmīti
2.1.2.43	pṛthivī vā annānāṃ śamayitrī tayaivainacchamayāṃcakāra
2.1.2.44	so 'bibhet prāśnantaṃ mā hiṃsiṣyatīti
2.1.2.45	agneṣ ṭvāsyena prāśnāmīty abravīt
2.1.2.46	na hy agner āsyaṃ kiṃcana hinasti
2.1.2.47	so 'bibhet prāśitaṃ mā hiṃsiṣyatīti

2.1.2.50	varuṇasyodara iti na hi varuṇasyodaraṃ kiṃcana hinastīti
2.1.3.1	atho āhur brāhmaṇasyodara iti
2.1.3.2	ātmāsyātmann ātmānaṃ me mā hiṃsīḥ svāheti
2.1.3.3	annaṃ vai sarveṣāṃ bhūtānām ātmā tenaivainacchamayāṃcakāra
2.1.3.4	prāśitam anumantrayate yo 'gnir nṛmaṇā nāma brāhmaṇeṣu praviṣṭas tasmin ma etat suhutam astu prāśitraṃ tan mā mā hiṃsīt parame vyoman iti
2.1.3.5	tat sarveṇa brahmaṇā prāśnāt
2.1.3.6	tata enaṃ nāhinat
2.1.3.7	tasmād yo brahmiṣṭhaḥ syāt taṃ brahmāṇaṃ kurvīta
2.1.3.8	bṛhaspatir vai sarvaṃ brahma
2.1.3.9	sarveṇa ha vā etad brahmaṇā yajñaṃ dakṣiṇata udyacchate
2.1.3.10	apa vā etasmāt prāṇāḥ krāmanti ya āviddhaṃ prāśnāti
2.1.3.11	adbhir mārjayitvā prāṇānt saṃspṛśate vāṅ ma āsyann iti
2.1.3.12	amṛtaṃ vai prāṇāḥ
2.1.3.13	amṛtam āpaḥ
2.1.3.14	prāṇān eva yathāsthānam upāhvayate
2.1.3.15	tad u haika āhur indrāya paryaharann iti
2.1.3.16	te devā abruvann indro vai devānām ojiṣṭho baliṣṭhaḥ
2.1.3.17	tasmā enat pariharateti
2.1.3.18	tat tasmai paryaharan
2.1.3.19	tat sa brahmaṇā śamayāṃcakāra
2.1.3.20	tasmād āhur indro brahmeti
2.1.3.21	yavamātraṃ bhavati
2.1.3.22	yavamātraṃ vai viṣasya na hinasti
2.1.3.23	yad adhastād abhighārayati tasmād adhastāt prakṣaraṇaṃ prajā arur na hinasti
2.1.3.24	yad upariṣṭād abhighārayati tasmād upariṣṭāt prakṣaraṇaṃ prajā arur na hinasti
2.1.3.25	yad ubhayato 'bhighārayaty ubhayato 'bhighāri prajā arur ghātukaṃ syāt

2.1.4.1	agreṇa pariharati
2.1.4.2	tīrthenaiva pariharati
2.1.4.3	vi vā etad yajñaś chidyate yat prāśitraṃ pariharati

2.1.4.5	sarveṇa ha vā etad brahmaṇā yajñaṃ dakṣiṇataḥ saṃdadhāti

2.2.6.11	aśvināv adhvaryū
2.2.6.12	tasmād adhvaryū gharmaṃ saṃbharataḥ
2.2.6.13	taṃ saṃbhṛtyocatur brahman gharmeṇa pracariṣyāmo hotar gharmam abhiṣṭuhy udgātaḥ sāmāni gāyeti
2.2.6.14	pracarata gharmam ity anujānāti
2.2.6.15	brahmaprasūtā hi pracaranti
2.2.6.16	brahma hedaṃ prasavānām īśe
2.2.6.17	savitṛprasūtatāyai
2.2.6.18	gharmaṃ tapāmi brahma jajñānam iyaṃ pitryā rāṣṭry etv agra iti gharmaṃ tāpyamānam upāsīta śastravad ardharcaśa āhāvapratigaravarjaṃ rūpasamṛddhābhiḥ
2.2.6.19	etad vai yajñasya samṛddhaṃ yad rūpasamṛddham
2.2.6.20	yat karma kriyamāṇam ṛg yajur vābhivadati svasti tasya yajñasya pāram aśnute ya evaṃ veda
2.2.6.21	devamithunaṃ vā etad yad gharmaḥ
2.2.6.22	tasmād antardhāya pracaranti
2.2.6.23	antarhitā vai mithunaṃ carantīti
2.2.6.24	tad etad devamithunam ity ācakṣate
2.2.6.25	tasya yo gharmas tacchiśnam
2.2.6.26	yau śaphau tāv āṇḍyau
2.2.6.27	yopayamanī te śroṇikapāle
2.2.6.28	yat payas tad retaḥ
2.2.6.29	tad agnau devayonyāṃ reto brahmamayaṃ dhatte prajananāya
2.2.6.30	so 'gnir devayonir ṛṅmayo yajurmayaḥ sāmamayo brahmamayo 'mṛtamaya āhutimayaḥ sarvendriyasampanno yajamāna ūrdhvaḥ svargaṃ lokam eti
2.2.6.31	tad āhur na prathamayajñe pravargyaṃ kurvītānupanāmukā ha vā enam uttare yajñakratavo bhavantīti
2.2.6.32	kāmaṃ tu yo 'nūcānaḥ śrotriyaḥ syāt tasya pravṛñjyāt
2.2.6.33	ātmā vai sa yajñasyeti vijñāyate
2.2.6.34	apaśirasā ha vā eṣa yajñena yajate yo 'pravargyeṇa yajate
2.2.6.35	śiro ha vā etad yajñasya yat pravargyaḥ
2.2.6.36	tasmāt pravargyavataiva yājayen nāpravargyeṇa
2.2.6.37	tad apy eṣābhyanūktā catvāri śṛṅgeti
2.2.7.1	devāś ca ha vā ṛṣayaś cāsuraiḥ saṃyattā āsan
2.2.7.2	teṣām asurāṇām imāḥ puraḥ pratyabhijitā āsann ayasmayī pṛthivī rajatāntarikṣaṃ hariṇī dyauḥ
2.2.7.3	te devāḥ saṃghātaṃ saṃghātaṃ parājayanta
2.2.7.4	te 'vidur anāyatanā hi vai smaḥ
2.2.7.5	tasmāt parājayāmahā iti
2.2.7.6	ta etāḥ puraḥ pratyakurvata havirdhānaṃ diva āgnīdhram antarikṣāt sadaḥ pṛthivyāḥ
2.2.7.7	te devā abruvann upasadam upāyāma
2.2.7.8	upasadā vai mahāpuraṃ jayantīti
2.2.7.9	ta ebhyo lokebhyo niraghnan
2.2.7.10	ekayāmuṣmāllokād ekayāntarikṣād ekayā pṛthivyāḥ
2.2.7.11	tasmād āhur upasadā vai mahāpuraṃ jayantīti
2.2.7.12	ta ebhyo lokebhyo nirhatā ṛtūn prāviśan
2.2.7.13	te ṣaḍ upāyan
2.2.7.14	tān upasadbhir evartubhyo niraghnan
2.2.7.15	dvābhyām amuṣmāllokād dvābhyām antarikṣād dvābhyāṃ pṛthivyāḥ
2.2.7.16	ta ṛtubhyo nirhatāḥ saṃvatsaraṃ prāviśan
2.2.7.17	te dvādaśopāyan
2.2.7.18	tān upasadbhir eva saṃvatsarān niraghnan
2.2.7.19	catasṛbhir amuṣmāllokāccatasṛbhir antarikṣāccatasṛbhiḥ pṛthivyāḥ
2.2.7.20	te saṃvatsarān nirhatā ahorātre prāviśan
2.2.7.21	te yat sāyam upāyaṃs tenainān rātryā anudanta yat prātas tenāhnaḥ
2.2.7.22	tasmād gauḥ sāyaṃ prātastanam āpyāyate prātaḥ sāyantanam
2.2.7.23	tān upasadbhir evaibhyo lokebhyo nudamānā āyan
2.2.7.24	tato devā abhavan parāsurāḥ
2.2.7.25	sarvebhya evaibhyo lokebhyo bhrātṛvyaṃ nudamāna eti ya evaṃ vidvān upasadam upaiti
2.2.8.1	na dvādaśāgniṣṭomasyopasadaḥ syuḥ
2.2.8.2	aśāntā nirmṛjyur na tisro 'hīnasya

2.2.9.1	atha yatrāhādhvaryur agnīd devapatnīr vyācakṣva subrahmaṇya subrahmaṇyām āhvayeti tad apareṇa gārhapatyaṃ prāṅmukhas tiṣṭhann anavānann āgnīdhro devapatnīr vyācaṣṭe

2.2.10.1	yathā vai ratha ekaikam aram abhipratitiṣṭhan vartata evaṃ yajña ekaikāṃ tanvam abhipratitiṣṭhann eti
2.2.10.2	purā pracaritor āgnīdhrīye hotavyāḥ
2.2.10.3	etaddha vā uvāca vāsiṣṭhaḥ sātyahavyo 'skan soma ity ukte mā sūrkṣata pracarata prātar vāvādyāhaṃ somaṃ samasthāpayam iti
2.2.10.4	nāsya soma skandati ya evaṃ vidvānt somaṃ pibati
2.2.10.5	sa ha sma vai sa āsandyām āsīnaḥ saktubhir upamathya somaṃ pibati
2.2.10.6	ahaṃ vāva sarvato yajñaṃ veda ya etān veda
2.2.10.7	na mām eṣa hiṃsiṣyatīti
2.2.10.8	nainaṃ somapītho na peyo hinasti ya evaṃ vidvānt somaṃ pibati
2.2.10.9	taṃ ha sma yad āhuḥ kasmāt tvam idam āsandyām āsīnaḥ saktubhir upamathya somaṃ pibasīti
2.2.10.10	devatāsv eva yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayāmīty abravīd brāhmaṇo yasyaivaṃ viduṣo yasyaivaṃ vidvān yajñārtyā yajñe prāyaścittaṃ juhoti
2.2.10.11	devatāsv eva yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
2.2.10.12	yajñārtiṃ pratijuhuyāt
2.2.10.13	sayonitvāya
2.2.10.14	trayastriṃśad vai yajñasya tanva iti

2.2.10.17	yajñaś caturthaḥ

2.2.10.20	devasya savituḥ prasave bṛhaspataye stuteti

2.2.11.1	devāś ca ha vā asurāś cāspardhanta
2.2.11.2	te devāḥ samāvad eva yajñe kurvāṇā āsan

2.2.11.4	te na vyāvṛtam agacchan
2.2.11.5	te devā abruvan nayatemaṃ yajñaṃ tira upary asurebhyas taṃsyāmaha iti
2.2.11.6	tam etābhir ācchādyodakrāman yajūṃṣi yajñe samidhaḥ svāheti
2.2.11.7	taṃ tira upary asurebhyo yajñam atanvata

2.2.12.1	yatra vijānāti brahmant somo 'skann iti tam etayālabhyābhimantrayate abhūd devaḥ savitā vandyo nu na idānīm ahna upavācyo nṛbhiḥ / vi yo ratnā bhajati mānavebhyaḥ śreṣṭhaṃ no atra draviṇaṃ yathā dadhad iti
2.2.12.2	ye agnayo apsv antar iti saptabhir abhijuhoti

2.3.9.1	prajāpatir vai yat prajā asṛjata tā vai tāntā asṛjata
2.3.9.2	tā hiṃkāreṇaivābhyajighrat
2.3.9.3	tāḥ prajā aśvam āraṃs tad badhyate vā etad yajño yaddhavīṃṣi pacyante yat somaḥ sūyate yat paśur ālabhyate
2.3.9.4	hiṃkāreṇa vā etat prajāpatir hatam abhijighrati yajñasyāhatatāyai yajñasyāptyai yajñasya vīryavattāyā iti
2.3.9.5	tasmād u hiṃkriyate
2.3.9.6	tasmād u ya eva pitā putrāṇāṃ sūrkṣati sa śreṣṭho bhavati
2.3.9.7	prajāpatir hi tam abhijighrati
2.3.9.8	yacchakunir āṇḍam adhyāste yan na sūyate taddhi sāpi hiṃkṛṇoti
2.3.9.9	atho khalv āhur maharṣir vā etad yajñasyāgre geyam apaśyat
2.3.9.10	tad etad yajñasyāgre geyaṃ yaddhiṃkāraḥ
2.3.9.11	taṃ devāś ca ṛṣayaś cābruvan vasiṣṭho 'yam astu yo no yajñasyāgre geyam adrāg iti
2.3.9.12	tad etad yajñasyāgre geyaṃ yaddhiṃkāraḥ
2.3.9.13	tato vai sa devānāṃ śreṣṭho 'bhavat
2.3.9.14	yena vai śreṣṭhas tena vasiṣṭhaḥ
2.3.9.15	tasmād yasmin vāsiṣṭho brāhmaṇaḥ syāt taṃ dakṣiṇāyā nāntarīyāt
2.3.9.16	tathā hāsya prīto hiṃkāro bhavati
2.3.9.17	atha devāś ca ha vā ṛṣayaś ca yad ṛksāme apaśyaṃs te ha smaite apaśyan
2.3.9.18	te yatraite apaśyaṃs tata evainaṃ sarvaṃ doham aduhan
2.3.9.19	te vā ete dugdhe yātayāme ye ṛksāme
2.3.9.20	te hiṃkāreṇaivāpyāyete
2.3.9.21	hiṃkāreṇa vā ṛksāme āpīne yajamānāya dohaṃ duhāte
2.3.9.22	tasmād u hiṃkṛtyādhvaryavaḥ somam abhiṣuṇvanti
2.3.9.23	hiṃkṛtyodgātāraḥ sāmnā stuvanti
2.3.9.24	hiṃkṛtyokthaśa ṛcārtvijyaṃ kurvanti
2.3.9.25	hiṃkṛtyātharvāṇo brahmatvaṃ kurvanti
2.3.9.26	tasmād u hiṃkriyate
2.3.9.27	prajāpatir hi tam abhijighrati
2.3.9.28	atho khalv āhur eko vai prajāpater vrataṃ bibharti gaur eva

2.3.23.4	atha haitat kevalam evendrasya yad ūrdhvaṃ marutvatīyāt

2.3.23.10	yad eva niṣkevalyāni tat svargasya lokasya rūpam
2.3.23.11	yad v eva niṣkevalyāni yā ha vai devatāḥ prātaḥsavane hotā śaṃsati tāḥ śastvā hotrāśaṃsino 'nuśaṃsanti maitrāvaruṇaṃ tṛcaṃ prauge hotā śaṃsati

2.3.23.13	aindraṃ tṛcaṃ prauge hotā śaṃsati
2.3.23.14	tad ubhayam aindram

2.3.23.16	aindrāgnaṃ tṛcaṃ prauge hotā śaṃsati

2.3.23.21	yad eva niṣkevalyāni tat svargasya lokasya rūpam
2.3.23.22	yad v eva niṣkevalyāni yaded adevīr asahiṣṭa māyā athābhavat kevalaḥ somo asyety ṛcābhyanūktam
2.3.23.23	devān ha yajñaṃ tanvānān asurarakṣāṃsy ajighāṃsan
2.3.23.24	te 'bruvan vāmadevaṃ tvaṃ na imaṃ yajñaṃ dakṣiṇato gopāyeti madhyato vasiṣṭham uttarato bharadvājaṃ sarvān anu viśvāmitram
2.3.23.25	tasmān maitrāvaruṇo vāmadevān na pracyavate vasiṣṭhād brāhmaṇācchaṃsī bharadvājād acchāvākaḥ sarve viśvāmitrāt

2.6.6.13	sa vā eka eva
2.6.6.14	tasmād ekasūktaḥ
2.6.6.15	tasya yad dvayāny ahāni bhavanti śītāny anyāny uṣṇāny anyāni tasmād dvyukthaḥ
2.6.6.16	ṛtavo vāva hotrāḥ
2.6.6.17	te vā ekaikam
2.6.6.18	tasmād ekokthāḥ
2.6.6.19	tad yad ekaikasyartau dvau dvau māsau bhavatas tasmād dvisūktāḥ
2.6.6.20	puruṣo vāva hotā
2.6.6.21	sa vā eka eva
2.6.6.22	tasmād ekasūktaḥ
2.6.6.23	sa yat puruṣo bhavaty anyathaiva pratyaṅ bhavaty anyathā prāṅ tasmād dvyukthaḥ
2.6.6.24	aṅgāni vāva hotrāḥ
2.6.6.25	tāni vā ekaikam
2.6.6.26	tasmād ekokthāḥ
2.6.6.27	tad yad ekaikam aṅgaṃ dyutir bhavati tasmād dvisūktāḥ
2.6.6.28	tad āhur yad dvyuktho hotaikasūkta ekokthā hotrā dvisūktāḥ kathaṃ tat samaṃ bhavati
2.6.6.29	yad eva dvidevatyābhir yajanty atho yad dvisūktā hotrā iti brūyāt
2.6.6.30	tad āhur yad agniṣṭoma eva sati yajñe dve hotur ukthe atiricyete kathaṃ tato hotrā na vyavacchidyanta iti
2.6.6.31	yad eva dvidevatyābhir yajanty atho yad dvisūktā hotrā iti brūyāt
2.6.6.32	tad āhur yad agniṣṭoma eva sati yajñe sarvā devatāḥ sarvāṇi chandāṃsy āpyāyayanty atha katamena chandasāyātayāmāny ukthāni praṇayanti kayā devatayeti
2.6.6.33	gāyatreṇa chandasāgninā devatayeti brūyāt
2.6.6.34	devān ha yajñaṃ tanvānān asurarakṣāṃsy abhicerire yajñaparvaṇi yajñam eṣāṃ haniṣyāmas tṛtīyasavanaṃ prati
2.6.6.35	tṛtīyasavane ha yajñas tvariṣṭo baliṣṭhaḥ
2.6.6.36	pratanumeṣāṃ yajñaṃ haniṣyāma iti
2.6.6.37	te varuṇaṃ dakṣiṇato 'yojayan madhyato bṛhaspatim uttarato viṣṇum
2.6.6.38	te 'bruvann ekaikāḥ smaḥ
2.6.6.39	nedam utsahāmaha iti
2.6.6.40	stuto dvitīyo yenedaṃ saha vyaśnavāmahā iti
2.6.6.41	tān indro 'bravīt sarve maddvitīyā stheti
2.6.6.42	te sarva indradvitīyāḥ
2.6.6.43	tasmād aindrāvāruṇam aindrābārhaspatyam aindrāvaiṣṇavam anuśasyate
2.6.6.44	dvitīyavanto ha vā etena svā bhavanti
2.6.6.45	dvitīyavanto manyante ya evaṃ veda
2.6.7.1	āgneyīṣu maitrāvaruṇasyokthaṃ praṇayanti
2.6.7.2	vīryaṃ vā agniḥ
2.6.7.3	vīryeṇaivāsmai tat praṇayanti
2.6.7.4	aindrāvāruṇam anuśasyate
2.6.7.5	vīryaṃ vā indraḥ
2.6.7.6	kṣatraṃ varuṇaḥ
2.6.7.7	paśava ukthāni
2.6.7.8	vīryeṇaiva tat kṣatreṇa cobhayataḥ paśūn parigṛhṇāti sthityā anapakrāntyai
2.6.7.9	aindrīṣu brāhmaṇācchaṃsina ukthaṃ praṇayanti
2.6.7.10	vīryaṃ vā indraḥ
2.6.7.11	vīryeṇaivāsmai tat praṇayanti
2.6.7.12	aindrābārhaspatyam anuśasyate
2.6.7.13	vīryaṃ vā indraḥ
2.6.7.14	brahma bṛhaspatiḥ
2.6.7.15	paśava ukthāni
2.6.7.16	vīryeṇaiva tad brahmaṇā cobhayataḥ paśūn parigṛhṇāti sthityā anapakrāntyai
2.6.7.17	aindrīṣv acchāvākasyokthaṃ praṇayanti
2.6.7.18	vīryaṃ vā indraḥ
2.6.7.19	vīryeṇaivāsmai tat praṇayanti
2.6.7.20	aindrāvaiṣṇavam anuśasyate
2.6.7.21	vīryaṃ vā indraḥ
2.6.7.22	yajño viṣṇuḥ
2.6.7.23	paśava ukthāni
2.6.7.24	vīryeṇaiva tad yajñena cobhayataḥ paśūn parigṛhya kṣatre 'ntataḥ pratiṣṭhāpayati
2.6.7.25	tasmād u kṣatriyo bhūyiṣṭhaṃ hi paśūnām īśate
2.6.7.26	yādhiṣṭhātā pradātā yasmai prattā vedā avaruddhāḥ
2.6.7.27	tāny etāny aindrāṇi jāgatāni śaṃsanti
2.6.7.28	atho etair eva sendraṃ tṛtīyasavanam etair jāgataṃ savanam
2.6.7.29	dharāṇi ha vā asyaitāny ukthāni bhavanti yan nābhānediṣṭho vālakhilyo vṛṣākapir evayāmarut
2.6.7.30	tasmāt tāni sārdham evopeyuḥ
2.6.7.31	sārdham idaṃ retaḥ siktaṃ samṛddham ekadhā prajanayāmeti
2.6.7.32	ye ha vā etāni nānūpeyur yathā retaḥ siktaṃ vilumpet kumāraṃ vā jātam aṅgaśo vibhajet tādṛk tat
2.6.7.33	tasmāt tāni sārdham evopeyuḥ
2.6.7.34	sārdham idaṃ retaḥ siktaṃ samṛddham ekadhā prajanayāmeti
2.6.7.35	śilpāni śaṃsati devaśilpāni
2.6.7.36	eteṣāṃ vai śilpānām anukṛtīha śilpam adhigamyate
2.6.7.37	hastī kaṃso vāso hiraṇyam aśvatarīrathaḥ śilpam
2.6.7.38	śilpaṃ hāsya samadhigamyate ya evaṃ veda
2.6.7.39	yad eva śilpāni śaṃsati tat svargasya lokasya rūpam
2.6.7.40	yad v eva śilpāny ātmasaṃskṛtir vai śilpāni
2.6.7.41	ātmānam evāsya tat saṃskurvanti
2.6.15.1	athāhanasyāḥ śaṃsati yad asyā aṃhubhedyā iti
2.6.15.2	āhanasyād vā idaṃ sarvaṃ prajātam
2.6.15.3	āhanasyād vā etad adhiprajāyate
2.6.15.4	asyaiva sarvasyāptyai prajātyai
2.6.15.5	tā vai ṣaṭ śaṃset
2.6.15.6	ṣaḍ vā ṛtavaḥ
2.6.15.7	ṛtavaḥ pitaraḥ
2.6.15.8	pitaraḥ prajāpatiḥ
2.6.15.9	prajāpatir āhanasyāḥ
2.6.15.10	tā daśa śaṃsed iti śāmbhavyasya vacaḥ
2.6.15.11	daśākṣarā virāṭ
2.6.15.12	vairājo yajñaḥ
2.6.15.13	taṃ garbhā upajīvanti
2.6.15.14	śrīr vai virāṭ
2.6.15.15	yaśo 'nnādyam
2.6.15.16	śriyam eva tad virājaṃ yaśasy annādye pratiṣṭhāpayati
2.6.15.17	pratitiṣṭhantīr idaṃ sarvam anupratitiṣṭhati
2.6.15.18	pratitiṣṭhati prajayā paśubhir ya evaṃ veda
2.6.15.19	tisraḥ śaṃsed iti vātsyaḥ
2.6.15.20	trivṛd vai retaḥ siktaṃ sambhavaty āṇḍam ulbaṃ jarāyu
2.6.15.21	trivṛtpratyayaṃ mātā pitā yaj jāyate tat tṛtīyam
2.6.15.22	abhūtodyam evaitad yac caturthīṃ śaṃset
2.6.15.23	sarvā eva ṣoḍaśa śaṃsed iti haike
2.6.15.24	kāmārto vai retaḥ siñcati
2.6.15.25	retasaḥ siktāt prajāḥ prajāyante prajānāṃ prajananāya
2.6.15.26	prajāvān prajanayiṣṇur bhavati prajātyai prajāyate prajayā paśubhir ya evaṃ veda
2.6.16.1	atha dādhikrīṃ śaṃsati dadhikrāvṇo akāriṣam iti
2.6.16.2	tata uttarāḥ pāvamānīḥ śaṃsati sutāso madhumattamā iti
2.6.16.3	annaṃ vai dādhikrī
2.6.16.4	pavitraṃ pāvamānyaḥ
2.6.16.5	tad u haike pāvamānībhir eva pūrvaṃ śastvā tata uttarā dādhikrīṃ śaṃsantīyaṃ vāg annādyā yaḥ pavata iti vadantaḥ
2.6.16.6	tad u tathā na kuryāt
2.6.16.7	upanaśyati ha vāg aśanāyatī
2.6.16.8	sa dādhikrīm eva pūrvaṃ śastvā tata uttarāḥ pāvamānīḥ śaṃsati
2.6.16.9	tad yad dādhikrīṃ śaṃsatīyaṃ vāg āhanasyāṃ vācam avādīt
2.6.16.10	tad devapavitreṇaiva vācaṃ punīte
2.6.16.11	sā vā anuṣṭub bhavati
2.6.16.12	vāg vā anuṣṭup
2.6.16.13	tat svenaiva chandasā vācaṃ punīte
2.6.16.14	tām ardharcaśaḥ śaṃsati pratiṣṭhityā eva
2.6.16.15	atha pāvamānīḥ śaṃsati
2.6.16.16	pavitraṃ vai pāvamānyaḥ
2.6.16.17	iyaṃ vāg āhanasyāṃ vācam avādīt
2.6.16.18	tat pāvamānībhir eva vācaṃ punīte
2.6.16.19	tāḥ sarvā anuṣṭubho bhavanti
2.6.16.20	vāg vā anuṣṭup
2.6.16.21	tat svenaiva chandasā vācaṃ punīte
2.6.16.22	tā ardharcaśaḥ śaṃsati pratiṣṭhityā eva
2.6.16.23	ava drapso aṃśumatīm atiṣṭhad ity etaṃ tṛcam aindrābārhaspatyaṃ sūktaṃ śaṃsati
2.6.16.24	atha haitad utsṛṣṭam
2.6.16.25	tad yad etaṃ tṛcam aindrābārhaspatyam antyaṃ tṛcam aindrājāgataṃ śaṃsati savanadhāraṇam idaṃ gulmaha iti vadantaḥ
2.6.16.26	tad u tathā na kuryāt
2.6.16.27	triṣṭubāyatanā vā iyaṃ vāg eṣāṃ hotrakāṇāṃ yad aindrābārhaspatyā tṛtīyasavane
2.6.16.28	tad yad etaṃ tṛcam aindrābārhaspatyam antyaṃ tṛcam aindrājāgataṃ śaṃsati sva evainaṃ tad āyatane prīṇāti svayor devatayoḥ
2.6.16.29	kāmaṃ nityam eva paridadhyāt
2.6.16.30	kāmaṃ tṛcasyottamayā
2.6.16.31	tad āhuḥ saṃśaṃset ṣaṣṭhe 'hani na saṃśaṃset
2.6.16.32	katham anyeṣv ahaḥsu saṃśaṃsati
2.6.16.33	katham atra na saṃśaṃsatīti
2.6.16.34	atho khalv āhur naiva saṃśaṃset
2.6.16.35	svargo vai lokaḥ ṣaṣṭham ahaḥ
2.6.16.36	asamāyī vai svargo lokaḥ
2.6.16.37	kaś cid vai svarge loke śamayatīti
2.6.16.38	tasmān na saṃśaṃsati
2.6.16.39	yad eva na saṃśaṃsati tat svargasya lokasya rūpam
2.6.16.40	yad v evaināḥ saṃśaṃsati yan nābhānediṣṭho vālakhilyo vṛṣākapir evayāmarud etāni vā atrokthāni bhavanti
2.6.16.41	tasmān na saṃśaṃsati
2.6.16.42	aindro vṛṣākapiḥ
2.6.16.43	sarvāṇi chandāṃsy aitaśapralāpaḥ
2.6.16.44	upāpto yad aindrābārhaspatyā tṛtīyasavane tad yad etaṃ tṛcam aindrābārhaspatyaṃ sūktaṃ śaṃsaty aindrābārhaspatyā paridhānīyā viśo adevīr abhyācarantīr iti
2.6.16.45	aparajanā ha vai viśo devīḥ
2.6.16.46	na hy asyāparajanaṃ bhayaṃ bhavati
2.6.16.47	śāntāḥ prajāḥ kﾱptāḥ sahante yatraivaṃvidaṃ śaṃsati yatraivaṃvidaṃ śaṃsatīti brāhmaṇam
